6a2(rgyud): ts+tshin+dan gnyis rdza jug dus dang nor pa rgyus brnangs te bdun nus// de lani 'o rab dbyes byas pa po'i tshwa cong/ rnams ni sprin dang 'brog par 'gyur// 'byung ba mang 'a'adu ga byed mams
6a3(rgyud): ri bong shar gi cha dang bzhin du'o// rgya mtsho zla bas cha snas mnyam pa'i mnyam la gnas rgyu ba sbyin bzhin 'brog/ sbyin pa kun gi lhag dus dang nyi mas sbyar ba cha thob na yang de bzhin no// de bzhin nyi ma
6a4(rgyud): dges nyi ma nang pa chu chod sbyin bya 'phrog par 'gyur// rig byed gis ni gang zhig ches sbyor bsal bar nor te gsum pa'i cha sres bya/ rgyu skar dus ni nang pa gsum bcas nyi ma'i sbyin pa longs spyo
6a5(rgyud): dbus nas dag par bya// lhag ma'i bya ba ci ltar dag la ro dus ri bong dman pa'i bya'i rkang pa rnams/ longs rtsa rnams sbyar nas mnga' dang yon tan ri bod kyis ni longs spyod dang bcas cha thob pa/ 
6a6(rgyud): nyi mar sbyin dang 'phrod par snod 'gro'i dbang gis gzhan dag tu ni dag pa med// nyi mar dus ro klu dang bcu dang drug po phyogs klu drug/ de dang nam mkha' bskyod thob pa// nyi mar sbyin dang 'phrod par sdod 'gro
6a7(rgyud): gis gzhan dag tu ni dag pa med// nyi mar dus ro klu dang bcu dang drug po phyogs klu drug/ pa mthar gyur nor dang sbyin pa byeng dang lho ru'o// zla ba drug ni phyogs kyi dbye bas zla ba 'pho ba'i nga
6a8(rgyud): byed cu nyi ma laches byin nas 'og tu ros rgyur bza' longs spyod kyis bsgres nas/ mngasan gyur ri bong mu tshan mar gyur te zla ba'i 'gyur ro mi dbang kyi// mig gis nges nga rje de ni ga'i
6b1(rgyud): byed pa 'das nas 'dun pa'i cha'i lhag ma'o// drug pa'i lo la klu bsres nam mkha' dang ni brgya mtsho rnams 'gyur klu'i sres pas sbyangs// ri zla ba mes ni rab bcad nam mkha' 'os spyar rtsal sngogs pa
6b2(rgyud): bcad// gnyis dang sum bcu gza' dang rtsa'i tshogs 'dir ldan lo 'pho zla ba'o// lug sngogs la ni gza' dang rtse rnams rim pos spyod pa bkod nas de bcu gnyis zla ri byung bu rigs byed skyon myang
6b3(rgyud): dang ri bong ri zla gsum pa la rig byed ma dang 'byung zla mig la dus rig byed mig mig ni drug par ro// zla drug mnga' ste zla ri dus me drug byed ri dang 'jig rten no// drug dang rig byed stong dang stong po mgo mtho
6b4(rgyud): nangs nya'i dus la nyi ma'o// zla drug 'phel bar 'gyur zhing 'bri bar 'gyur ba mnyin mtshan la nyim skyabs nyi ma la rgyu bas temal rgyamatsho srog ste me'i chu sring nyin bzhin dus su 'phel 'gro
6b5(rgyud): bgrod ba'i yan lag gis/ ra na macan mo 'drel bar 'gyur te/ gangs ro'i byang du nyin pa'o// slab kyims ces banig+sa kris rnam bgrangs sbyi 'chos kyig skyes/ 
6b6(rgyud): chu gter gas bcad thub lhag gis bgrangs mkha' sogs chal skar ma ste/ lhag ma drug bcus gang sbyar sngar ga chu tshod de rnams/ chu srang gis ni de rnams sbyar thob pas rba bor lo dmar po gdon
6b7(rgyud): 'gyur zhing mun can dam rgyu skar phyed sres pa'o// zla ba sum bcus sbyar ba nyin bzhin dang bcas ri mkhan ra 'is thob pa ni// gsum gsum dbus su rnam par bsres kyang brgya mtsho ro yis thob drim ma/ 
6b8(rgyud): mam pa nyin mo'o// dus cig bris gsal ba'i nyin tshogs radang kyi hrI/ dus rnams kyis rnye cad// lcags kyu skar gis sbyar sngar yang ma las ros 'grog pa so ma tho myong
7a1(rgyud): yis dgra ni spyang bya gal te sbyin lag 'khor lo dang sres rnam dag bya// 'khor lo phyed dor phyed las kyang ni// lhag gyur lhag par dag ni rim min 'gyur
7a2(rgyud): 'gyur 'byung ba me dang zla ba bcad// gang thob dam pa'i las la ner sbyin rim pa dang rim pas so// de nyid bco brgyad ri dang gsal bar ro skong 'khor lo phyed de 'og tu lang
7a3(rgyud): tan ri bong gis ni 'khor lo phyed las thob// shar char bzung ba 'dod 'gyur rkang pa'i dbang gis gzhan gis cha la dar ba nyid// zos pa gong cig byas nas bza'i rnams 'gro ba'idapying kyi
7a4(rgyud): brtsol// de nas nyi mas skyes rnam par sbyang ste bla ma dag dang nyi skyes yang ni myur ba'i sa la'o// zla bu dkar pos nyi ma nges par nor 'gyur myur du bya ba'i rim pas song 'dir ni/ gze'i rgyu
7a5(rgyud): yis ni lhag ma rtsa rnams sbyar/ drug bcu chas thob rnams rgyu'i dbang gis gzung dang 'phrog pa de bzhin no// zos pa gong cig byas nas bza' 'gro'i dpung gis mu lu su sbyin dang 'phrog par
7a6(rgyud): rgyal ba la sogs gsal po shed bu'i rkang pa ma lus dkod par bya// de ltar gza' kun la ni rim pa yongs bgrangs rig par bya'o mi dbang kye/ zla bu dkar pos nyin phyed na mas dag 'gyur te zla buM
7a7(rgyud): spyod las/ ma lus nyin mo'i tshogs ni stong pa nam mkha' zla bgrangs me he ri yis dman// ri dang phug pa'iri dang klu yis 'phrogs pa yang sbyar lhag ma skar rdzogs dbye bas so// brjod pa'i cha lus
7a8(rgyud): chu tshod zla dbus longs spyod du 'gyur ro// zla bu nyi dbus pa ta nas rgyal po bor zhing rgyu skar byed ni yang dag rgyal bzang kye// lhag ma'i bya ba ci ltar dgar gyur nor dang sbyin pa dal dang gyur ba'i ci srasa?
7b1(rgyud): bya bar bcurare me stong myur ba'i bya bar rgyal sngogs so// nyin ma gong bu byas nas dal ba'i bya ba'i rkang pa rnams slar yang mkha' dang / nam mkha' ro mnyam mig gis mnan so me rgya mtshos bcad// lhag ma rgyu skar gis
7b2(rgyud): sbyar skar slar yang chu tshod dman pa'i bya bar bla ma'o// rgyu skar nyi mas dag bya drag rgu me ni dal ba'i bya ba'i rkang pa rnams slar yang myur ba'i rkang rnams gsal bar shed bu'i gnas su phyogs rgya ngo la srogs de rnams
7b3(rgyud): mikhar zlas nyin zhag sbyar nas chu gter nor gis dman bya 'iri rgyal mag gis bcad// rgyu skar gis sbyar longs spyod slar yang chu tshod myur ba'i bya bar sbal ba'i 'o// rgyu skar dus ni nyi mas dag bya mad 'a dus ri dong pa
7b4(rgyud): ba'i bya bar rkang rnams so// myur ba de nyid sngogs dbyes gsol bar shed bu'i rkang la ci ltar dgra la sbyin 'phrog go// gsol pa'i nyan tshogs kha mag rgyad dang rig byed kyis dman ro drug ri mkha' ci mkha' cig gis
7b5(rgyud): ni// bcad pa rgyu skar gis sgyu skar 'gyur spen par bco brgyad 'byung bar bya// rkang pa nyi shu rtsa gnyis zhig dus gsal bar ro rkang myur ba'i bya bar ro sogs so// myur dang ngal ba'i rgyu ba'i rim pa rkang 'gro dgo// 'khyogs
7b6(rgyud): nyid gis ni rim min pas de shar dang nub kyi phyogs la nyi ma 'gro ba'i dbang gis gza' rnams 'byung ba'o// zla ba bza' bzung sum bcu bdun ni lag pas du ba'i myur dang 'khyog pa'o// gang zhig nyi ma'i longs
7b7(rgyud): rab tu bzhugs par gza' de nges par nub par 'gyur// nyi ma por nas shar 'gyur bgrod par 'gro ba'i dbye bas de'i lam yin no// g.yon pa'i lam la gnas nyi 'gro ba'i dbang gis gza' rnams ju
7b8(rgyud): de ni byang du 'gro'i// g.yas gnas lho yis gsal bar yang ni phan tshun dag dag dang ni 'di thob po// rang bzhin yang dag gnas lA gal+ye dgrar gyur de ni nges par 'thob mo'o// rgyu skar phan tshun pa
7b9(rgyud): brtsod na de ru phan tshun du ni rig pa nyams// g.yon tu gal te zla ba bzhugs gyur nyi ma yang ni byang nis 'byung bar 'gyur// g.yon tu rtse mo 'phar gyur rgyalam bgrod pa'i dbang gis lho dang lho ru'i/ 
8a1(rgyud): na na sa du sa sa pa / rgyun sa spyang smra smra nga ga sa gan gzhan la
8a2(rgyud): 'dzin zhing 'byung ba rgyab tu yang // tha skar srogs dang nas nag phyed par nyin mtshan mnyam pa dbus su// 'og la'i ri mo'o// rgyu skar g.yas min nges par srid pa'i gnas su 'bru'i dbye bas yang dag bla
8a3(rgyud): gzhu'i rnam par dus 'brur mar me'i dkyil 'khor la gnas g.yas su 'ag la'i dbus gnas so// de ni g.yon tu gsil ba'i ri ste pad 'dab bza' ltar lu skyon srang la stsogs// me nas bsil bya
8a4(rgyud): nananam mkha' mkha' dang mda' klu'i ni dpag tshad stong // dbus su 'khor lo phyed kyis ri mos nyi ma yang // 'gro mtshan mo cig ni mnyam pa'o// phyi nas g.yas dang g.yas min rgyu zhing nyin mtshan rgyu sgra
8a5(rgyud): rim pas so// lami rnams mkha' dang klu zla dor zhing nyin mtshan la ni ji srid dgrod pa'i mtha'// nyi zla'i 'grib dang 'phel ba drug bcas 'phel ba nyi nges par nyin mtshan dag ni drug bcu ma/ grangs
8a6(rgyud): mi rnams kyi ni 'phro ba mnyam 'gyur lug nyid srang gi nyi ma'o// de nas nyid brgyad dus bur khyu mchog la gnas sdig pa la de bzhin no// bu ga zhes bya med grangs la theg po lacug nas phyogs kyi
8a7(rgyud): nya mad dkar ka tar gnas yang ni chu srin la gnas lnga pa bcu gcig par song ga bum par bzhugs pas bcu gnyis ro sa ra nya dang bu mo la gnas pa// 'dir ni gauyon/ 
8a8(rgyud): chu srin la gnas bum pas nyi mar gnyis pa'o// nya dang dam bu gsum par skrod pa mi rnams lug dang nyi ma bzhi par ro// 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i nyi ma khyo mchog gnas
8a9(rgyud): pa drug bdun pa la// nyi ma kar ka ta ra gnas gyur pa seng ge la gnas pa'i dum bu brgyad pa la// bu mo bug par srang gnyis 'gyur zhing bcu pa sdig pa drag po ru dum bya/ 
8b1(rgyud): bcu gnyis la 'gyur bgrod pa mi rnams la yang bcu gnyis brtsibs kyi sa ru'o// de ltar g.yas pa yin zhing nyi mgro dbang gis kar ka tar/ ba sogs 'bru lnga'o// steng du drug dang klu'i grangs
8b2(rgyud): gsungs te byang gi smod pa'i mtha' ru'o// de nas zang de g.yas 'gyur drag po'i grangs kyis stong phrag rnams so mi dbang kye// stong phrag brgya bcu rtsa gcig mda'i rgyas dman yi dbus
8b3(rgyud): ng+ge ba ga dang ga gyugs nams mkha' dang dang du byung dang marnas lu nas byed sto ba
8b4(rgyud): sa byang du byung la gnas pam+b+ha/ na ni chas rnams kyis 'gyur phyogs kyis degro 'dro dadangagacad dgan stong drug sa// khye bcas masu gu zas tho snyen dang bad rdzog na
8b5(rgyud): stong phrag las// nyi ma 'bum gcig la gnas ma lus dus tshogs zla ba dang ni phyogs byed do// dum bu dum bur zla 'gyur sa stengs bcu gnyis rtsi rim pas so// tshang gang dumakhru gang 'gyur nyi ma
8b6(rgyud): gis 'dun pa'i mtshan mor de yin no// 'bum 'phrag gsum las lam la ni nyin mo zla 'gyur sa stengs bcu gnyis rtsi rim bdun du nyi ma'i rgyab tu mtshan ma'o// skye bo kun gi byang nas ri'i rgyal
8b7(rgyud): dbyang kye// nyi ma shar nas 'char zhing ri mnyam bgrod pa nub pa nub pa nyid yin no// dus dang thun 'tshams bzhi dang thun tshod dag ni nyin mtshan rtag tu yang drug rgyu// ri rab phyogs dang kas su
8b8(rgyud): tonyi ma'i sA la dus 'byor rnams kyi dbye bas phye// rtsang dus rkang pa drug bcas dpag tshad dag ni stong phrag rnams su nyi ma 'khor// drug bcu me'i 'bum phrag nyin mo 'khyer te lnga dang ri bo'i stong
8b9(rgyud): 'og la'i phyed nas mkha' me rtsa 'bab nyin mtshan 'phel ba dang ni 'grib pa'i lnga 'gro la ni g.yas dang g.yas min nyin mtshan re re ni dbus bzung srang gsum// lug gi dus 'byor sa
9a1(rgyud): dgu lag ste mkha' dus mig ni khyu mchog la// bzung gi na mkha' mkha' dang gnyis mang ro'i chu tshod yin te rigs ldan seng ge'o// bu mo'i drug dang byed bcas su 'gyuraringes par srang rtsogs/ 
9a2(rgyud): thams cad rims man pas// de bzhin nub tu dus 'byor de drug 'char ba yang ni rgyu skar dbye bas nyi ma'o// stong phrag nyi shu gcig dang ro rgya dang bcas 'byung zhing so'i cha rnams kyis// lus la
9a3(rgyud): dbugs lhag gang zhig nyin bzhin dus su 'byung ba ri dang dus kyi bgrangs// stong phrag sum bcu rtsa drug gis bgrags la brgya brgya'i tshong du rab tu grangs stong des mas ni rab bcad chu tshod 'ang
9a4(rgyud): 'gyur drug bcu cha yis nyin mtshan no// zla ba'i phyogs de nyi ma'i bgrod pa'i saM skyes zla ba dgu dang mtshan mo'o// bla ma'i lo drug yin te sbal ba'i grong yin bgrod pa zla bre'i bu la'o// tshe zhes
9a5(rgyud): lo ni nyi mu'i mun pa can gris dgu de bzhin du bas mnan pa rgyal po kye// de ni thams cad gcig spus nor grangs pa'i dus lo phyed dang bcas pa zla gsum mo// grangs ni phyed dang bcas pa
9a6(rgyud): nyin mo los rgyar 'gyur zhing dus kyi 'khor los dman// srog rnams snying stobs 'bab dang rdul dang mun pa ru lus ngag sems kyi dbye bas so// de nas ji ltar 'gyur mtshan mo phyed dang tha
9a7(rgyud): pa'i nyin mo grangs ni phyed dang bcas pa'i nyin mo grangs 'di shin du nges par rab grags 'gyur ba dus kyis 'khor lo mi dbang kye// dus 'khor ma bcad bgrod pa skyed pa dgu na ma lus po na
9a8(rgyud): bkod par bya// bkra shis la sogs bza' lnga'i myur ba'i las la rgyu ba'i chu tshod ni// sa skyes rig+hi byed dus me rab tu 'gyur srong po'i gnas su rgyu ba'i dbye bas so// shar dang gzhan su phyed
9a9(rgyud): spyan dang nor gnas gnas kyi dbye bas sbyar bar bya// dang po rgyal dbang grangs kyis chu tshong rab 'gyur ma mig rnam pa gsum du'o// gnas min gcig bco brgyad chos dang drag me'i rtsibs dag po
9b1(rgyud): sum bcu rtsa rgyang rgya bcu gnas pa srid pa'i rkang pa la gnas lnga bcu gsum byocas 'dar// de la nyi ma rnam dag sbyin drang nor ni rim dang ma yin pas/ rig byed bug pa zla grangs chu tshod 'gyur zhing myur ba'i bya
9b2(rgyud): bar gza' lag gi// gnas gnyis drug bcu bzhan ni chos dang byed bu mos byas drag po dbyang chu ba'o// rtsa ba las ni rig byed drag po nges bcwo bcu gnyis pal na nyi shu'o// nye'u brgyad dang som pa
9b3(rgyud): bzhi shed bu'i gan su yang dag gnas pas rgyu dbye bas/ rgya mtsho dang ni nam mkha' zla grangs chu tshong gong bu 'dir 'gyur slar bu'o// gnas gnyis phyog chang dgu nor dus drug lag zla gyi las
9b4(rgyud): bug pa drag po thub pa rgyu kun rim pa yis ne mi dbang kye/ myur dang dam pa 'khyog pa yang ni gza' tshogs nges par nyi ma'i dbye bas 'gyur// drug zla rgya mtsho'i grangs ni chu tshod 'gyur zhing myur ba'i bya ba'o
9b5(rgyud): gnas gsum nyi shu lnga ste rgyal ba'i gnyis zhes de bzhin lag gnyis ni yin// skyon ches rgyad kyis rtsa ba drug dang namatha' yon tan gcig gis dman pa rgyu// mtha' ru me re gnas sred pa'i// noganas su su
9b6(rgyud): rgyu ba rim pas so// ny-i mu'i drug dang 'byung ba'i grangs 'gyur chu ched gong bu 'di nyid me dbang kyi// drug dang 'byung ba rig byed du ter me gzung stong ba'i phyed kyi rtsa las/ phyogs dang rerig byed 'byung ba'i dang / 
9b7(rgyud): nor me rim pa yis ni dgod par bya// de ltar dus 'khor ma lus pa ni nges par gzi brjing rgyu bar 'gyur de'o// su mo bcu rtsa drug phyed bcas zla ba nges par nongs drangs dral ba'i bya ba'i rkang pa'o// mgu dug min
9b8(rgyud): grangs rab 'gyur chu tshod kra shris la stsogs gza' rnams kyi/ shar dang nub tu de nyid bco brgyad bcu dang rig gnas po bu'o// phyogs dang dus me gza' lag gi ste rgu bcas me ni bla ma'i shar bcas nub tu'o// ba sangs
9b9(rgyud): madra' dang rgya mtsho slar 'gyur spen pa'i mig dang bcas pa myig nyon dus/ zla bar sa bu'i chu long spyod chu tshod dgu m+b+ha bcu lnga dang 'jig rten zla ba'i grangs kha ba sangs kyi 'di ltar gas tshig gi yang 'khor rI mo ste gong
10a1(rgyud): gnyen zhes gcig 'gyur sum lnga ba de nyid byed bcas zla ba mig dang bcas// tso bo long skyong nyin rnams nyin bzhin skye ba gza' longs spyod do// zla gcig dman pa'i 'ad pa zhes
10a2(rgyud): lhag 'gyur gza' rnams gang ma zos// de bas nges par byed bcas bdun ni gsal bar chu tshod leng spyod zla ba'i 'di nyid la// sgro gcan zla ba'i long spyod nyid bcas ri bo nang pa rtsa phyed kyis ni rnamapa
10a3(rgyud): dman// gsum ni nyi ma'i bgrod rdzogs ri bong 'dod pa'i zhag la zla ba'i rtsa lnga'o// gang yang rtsa phyed ma zos dus dang nyin mtshan dus su chare zla bas dman// de ni nyi ma'i lhag ma yin te// 
10a4(rgyud): grangs nyi zla'i nyin de bzhin no// sgra gcan zla ba 'i long skyong mig gis rnam grangs phyogs kyis long spyod kyis bcad las// thob pa du ba'i rtsa rnams nyin bzhin dus su zla bas khyod sa na
10a5(rgyud): skra gcan gis phyed bcas su srang bdun phrogs nges par don tan gas bgrangs nyi snod las dag bya// du ba byem rnams rgyu bdun dang rgyab du myur dang 'khyog du'o// rgyub sa
10a6(rgyud): sa shes 'gyur da na po'i spyo sa ngas so// gas drug gis ni kyi chod des rgya'adag rten chos kyi/ sa sgyu/ byed bsas dang rtsa gnyis can pazhin du
10a7(rgyud): myur dang 'khyog pa mdun dang rgyar ngu'o// ci srid phyed bcas zla ba de nyid ni shar gyur mo'i 'jig rten drug tu nyams// slar yang gal te dpal ldan dus kyi 'khor de bzhugs lo'i long spyod kyis mi ma
10a8(rgyud): de shar che shes zhes de shar yang ni mtha' med dus so// lo'i nyin mo lngas bgrangs slar yang 'das sbyar bgrod pa'i nyin mos rab tu dman// bug sregs 'gyur te gza' rnams dkyil 'khor rang 'gro yon
10b1(rgyud): tan dbang gis so// sa bu'i ri klu drug gi nyin tshogs 'gyur te bu ge ri lu ni// zla bu'i sau me rig byed 'gyur zhing lha'i bla ma'i sbal bu'i ri dang rgyal ba mig/ drug drug ri mkha' gcig ni nyin
10b2(rgyud): tshogs dkyil 'khor ni bu'i min// ri dus gcig nas dri'i nges bu nor 'gyur rta bu'i rgyas 'gyur rten tshigs bcus dazungs kyi'i ris panan sna du'o/ rgya tsho brgyad kyis pa
10b3(rgyud): skyong pa nam mkha' lag cu zung sngags pa nyi shu bu'i skyon yin no// sa bu'i phyed bcas dgur so// byed lhag rgyal po bza' lag ni rgyu skar nyi me ris dman sul bu'i nyi ma yin// ba ba sangs drug
10b4(rgyud): rjes sa sa so la sa ba nga gis sa ga nas se byung gA
10b5(rgyud): 'gro ba nyi ma'i dbus so// zla ba'i drug gis zla spyod dgrangs 'gyur dus kyi 'khor lo dang zla ba yis/ chos thob sbyin yin nyi dang ri bong gos ni rtsa phyid rjes su ma
10b6(rgyud): pa dus kyi slar yang ga lha gnyin bzhin dus su zla ba'i nyin mos dgrang bar bya// drug bcu nas rtsa nyin bzhin dus su myur dang 'khyog pa 'byung ba la// zla ba sngags par myur
10b7(rgyud): 'khyog pa'i rgyu bar rab bzhugs pa'o// ngal ba'i g.yas phyogs yin te rang 'gro yon tani dbang gis 'byung bar bya phyogs pas// zla ba'i gang zhig nyin mtshan sum bcu chu gter gyi sa
11a1(rgyud): sa bu mi 'dod shar des gal te slar yang smin drug sbyor nyid 'gyur ba'o// de la g.yul dang nang du gal te gyur na mi rnams dang po'i dbyangs mchi'o// bzang mo zla bus gnyis pa zhes bya/ 
11a2(rgyud): mngag sbyor nyid bza' de la// rgyu skar rgyal por gal te bla mar 'gyur na gsum pa dag ni shi bar 'gyur// stong tshes pa sangs gal te mon grus 'gyur na bzhi pa ru ni shi bar 'gyur// grang ba dman pa
11a3(rgyud): bcas po pra nyer rab 'gyur lnga pa mo ni shi bar 'gyur// nyims rga shar rnams la shi ba'i sbyor bas rnam bral 'bras bu mang bar 'gyur// nang dang 'thab mo 'gron 'grong bag len dge dang mi dge ba'i byas
11a4(rgyud): bu shes par bya// de ltar rgyu skar gza' dang dbyangs sogs chos rnams de nyid lnga'i rab dbye bas// phyogs dang zla ba bgrod lo drug bcu'i lo 'di'u ni shar bar 'gyur// sgyid sogs ldan
11a5(rgyud): lag bcu gnyis kyis 'di shar gyur phyogs kyi dbye ba nyid do// nyin mo bdun bcu rtsa gnyis 'di shar 'gyuradabyangs rnams zla ba'i dbye bas so// zla ba drug gis ni
11a6(rgyud): bgrod pa'i cha ster rab 'gyur skor// tshe lo bcu gnyis kyi lo yin no// de ltar dbyangs lnga 'dir shar gyur na phyi nas yang ni nub par 'gyur// dang po dbyangs rnams byis pa yin zhing rang chetshes yon
11a7(rgyud): tan dbangs gis dpal dang gzhon nu gnyis pa la// dar ba rgan mo rim gris me dang chu gter nyin mo lnga pa la ni nub par 'gyur// a srogs dbyangs lnga gang yin nges par yon tan gis grangs nyis
11a8(rgyud): lnga'i rab dbye bas rang rnams nag po'i phyogs las de ni nges par 'gyur te/ skyed dang sdud pa'i sbyor ba yis// rgyu skar nyi shu bdun gang nyi ma'i dus 'byor gsal bar ram de'i chu tshod cha dgu'o// / 
11b1(rgyud): 'di rnams rang bzhin gsum po g.yo btan shin du mnyam pa lus kyis dus 'byor srogs 'dir ro// lug dang kar ka srang des chu srin 'dir rgyu de yis dman pa btan pa rnams yin no// lhag ma gzhan pa'i
11b2(rgyud): rang bzhin gnyis te nyin bzhin dus su rtag par de rnams shar// de la bdud tsam sum bcu'i nyin mo'i dus su rtsa yang drug bcu nyid yin no// dang po dbyangs ni sum bcu 'dir shar gyur na nges par yud tsam
11b3(rgyud): sde yig sum bcu la ni chu tshod rab 'gyur thung dang ring po'i dbye bas so// tshes chad dang ni zla ba'i dbus su 'char bar brjod par brjod de de nas nub par 'gyur ba yin// stong pa rlung dang me chu gzhan yang
11b4(rgyud): sa ni dbyangs lnga dang po rigs yin no// sgra gcan me zla bu'i sbal pa bla ma mi srun nyi bu'i 'dir ni lhag pa'i lha// sngon brjod dus 'byor re re nyin mo dbang gis rtsa rnams de ru sgrub par bya// 
11b5(rgyud): de bus dbyangs gang 'gyur te bza' 'dir stobs ldan de'i dkyil 'khor dag ni sgrub par bya// g.yon 'dir dbyangs rnam sa thung ru 'gyur te g.yos pa ru ni gzhan rnams so// g.yon du
11b6(rgyud): stong srogs de nyid brda' srogs sgra gcan gtso bo ma lus pa// g.yos su sa sogs de nyid sa sogs par nye bu la srogs nyid kyis so// bya'am dus kyi rtsa ni gza'i srid pa dang mnyam dbyangs dang bcas pa
11b7(rgyud): sgrub par bya// zhu ba g.yul gyi dus su dus kyi stong par shar bas rab tu 'chi bar 'gyur ba yin// rlung la nyi mas bcom dang rma ru 'gyur te me dang sa bus shar bas so// dum po chu dang bla mas hU~M
11b8(rgyud): zhings dang dman pa shar ba g.yul du mi 'gyur ro// shi dang nyon mongs rma dang 'de ba mnyam zhing zhu ba po dang nad pa la// sgra gcan stong par shar bas g.yul du gra ni nges par nyams par
12a1(rgyud): 'gyur dag zla bas bcom te rdza bu me dag shar rabs g.yul du rma dag 'byung ba sangs chu yis nor 'thob dgra yang dbang 'gyur ba dang du bar shar bas so// 'di ltar 'grong dang byug
12a2(rgyud): ma len par dga' ba'i 'bras bur 'gyur te g.yon lam gza' rnams kyis// pho nyas dbyangs gang nges par bcus bgrangs dus kyi 'khor lo drang sres pa// slar yang 'byung bas de sbyar de rnaMs
12a3(rgyud): nye ba'i ming ldan bdun chas lhag pa rnams// zla ba me dang mda' re mi mnyam gnas par song bas mi rnams la ni 'grub pa med// mig dang reg byed ro ni shin du mnyam pa'i gnas nas nges par
12a4(rgyud): dgongs pa 'grub/ lo rnams zla ba phyogs dang nyin dang mtshan du dus 'byor dbus su rab tu zhugs// dus 'byor gcig ni dbye bas lnga yis gzi' tshes dang ldan dbyangs cas
12a5(rgyud): de nyid kyis tha dad // de nyid gcig ni dbugs ni drug bcus lhag pa'i phrag yon tan dus kye rtsal gnas// rba'i cha ni sra chu srong yin bzhin de'i cha shes zhes bya dbu gos drug
12a6(rgyud): mi dbang kye// dbus 'byung 'jug pa'i dus su dge dang mi dge'i 'bras bu rnal 'byor ldan pas shes par byos// ltas shes dus rtsar gnas pa'i nyi ma'i dbang gis// zla ba nyi ma'i sgrub byas
12a7(rgyud): la'o// da ltar byung ba shes par dge mi dge'i 'bras bu 'jig rten 'di ru gang gis brjod// long ba des ni long ba bzung nas glang chen seng ges gang ba'i cha nag tshul 'jug par byed// phra ma'i rnal 'byor
12a8(rgyud): ma shes nam bza' stobs dang bcas dus 'byor ba sbyin par bya// dus med nyi mas skyes shing byed bu skye ba bdun dus gnas la ni// mchi nang rma dang ma lus nor ni nges par ru ni de la nyams par byed/ 
12b1(rgyud): de phyir de ni stang bya nges par bdag gis tshig gis dus 'byor gzhan ma rab sbyin bya// sgra gcan zla ba zla bu'i bla ma sbal pas skyes pa bdun dus la gnas na// dgra nyams rgyas pa g.yul du rnam rgyal rje/ 
12b2(rgyud): ni bud med dang bcas nor 'thob po// yang dag dus 'byor kun gis gal te yang ni rang gi lus la g.yon gi rtsar gyur na// nges par kun 'grub ma lus sa stengs gnas su dag pa'i gza' dang chos kyis
12b3(rgyud): so/ rgyu skar cha gsum bya zhing chu chu skye ba'i rgyu skar dang po'o// mi mnyam rkang pa la gnas drug rnams zla ba dang bcas nges par nad pa rnams na mchi// tha skar tshogs kyis rtsa gsum la ni sprul bzhin
12b4(rgyud): kyang rgyan ci srinam gru'i bar du'o// sdig pa'i zla ba skye ba'i skur gyur ma rnams rtsa gcig de ldan ni nyams par 'gyur ro// drug ces rgyad ri zla ba bcu dang dgu bcas bcu nye lo bzang
12b5(rgyud): nyi shu gcig/ nyi zla dag dang gza' lag bla ma klu dang dkar po de rnams rim par zos// de nas nad kyi gnas skabs slar yang de la sde brgyad yig rnams kyis ni// drag po rnams
12b6(rgyud): kyis ni min byed sde mchog tu byed dri ma byed gza' gang mdzes gzugs pa// dgun zla 'bring po ma rig chu srin bum pa'i nyi ma dag dang // dgun zla tha chungs la 'du byed skyed zla ra ba'i nya
12b7(rgyud): mas 'gyur zhing rnam shes mi dbang kye// sbrid zla 'bring dang tha chungs lug dang khyu mchog la gnas ming gzugs mag sngogs dang // dbyar zlar 'bring 'khrig pa kar ka tA'i tshes la reg pa tshor dram
12b8(rgyud): dbyar chung ston zla rab seng ge bu me tshes la srid pa nye bar len// ston zla 'bring po tha chungs srang dang sdig pa'i tshes la sred pa skye ba dang // dgu zla ra ba'i tshes la de bzhin gzhug nas rim pas
13a1(rgyud): 'gro gnyis dbang gis so// dgun 'bring dgun chung mtshams su nyi ma chu srin la gnas gza' der ma rig pa'o// de nas shi ba gnyis par 'gyur zhing 'di ltar skye ba gsum par
13a2(rgyud): mi dbang kye// 'di ltar sred sogs thams cad rim pas yongs bgrangs ji srid yan lag bcu gnyis so// de bas phyi'i cho ga 'gro gnyis dbang gis rgya lam yan lag drug pa'o// 
13a3(rgyud): phyogs dang tshes zhes bya gza' la nyi ma rgyu ba'i dbang gis rgyalam yan lag bcu drug la// 'du byed chu 'bring 'tshams su nyi ma bum pa la gnas ni 'du byed nyid// de'i nyon mo gnyis
13a4(rgyud): bar rnam shes 'gyur zhing ming dang gzugs ni gsum pa la// 'di ltar zla ba gnyis kyis yan lag 'gyur te nyi ma'i dbang skye dang sdud pa'i sbyor bas so// 'di ru ma rin
13a5(rgyud): la sogs yan lag mi mnyam 'gyur te/ zla ba thams cad dge ba'o// 'du byed la sogs mnyam pa gang zhi/ ga 'gron bgod bge len rtog par mi bgyi'o// 'di
13a6(rgyud): ltar phyogs kyi dbye ba ri bong can 'gro ba'i dbang gris yan lag bcu gang rnams so// kAr dang nag po'i phyogs la dang po'i chos kyi dbang dang skye dang sdud pa'i sbyor bas so// 
13a7(rgyud): nyi ma bkru shis du bya'i nang pa g.yas dang rgyab tu gnas na dgra ni rab tu 'joms par byed// g.yon dang mdun du gza' ba'i gzog ma lus zhi ba'i tshul gris ngo bzhin 'thub pa'i sad/ 
13a8(rgyud): rnal 'byor ma dang ko'u rlung byas drag pos g.yas dang rgyab tu mdzes pa ster// gnas stobs gnyis pa'i gzugs ni mnyam dang mi mnyam la gnas stobs gnyis bsod par byed// tshangs mo drag
13b1(rgyud): mo gzhon nu ma dang mkha' 'gro'i bdag 'gro phag mo rdo lag tsa mun ta dang dpal gyur nor ches dang po'i mtshams dang dgu pa la// nor sbyin mtshams lha min gshin rje chu dang rlung dbang tshes phyed la
13b2(rgyud): dpal mo// de rnams shar byed slar yang tshes rnams la ni brgyad gnyis dbye bas rnam thar dang // ke'u kang kar po'i phyogs l-i shar dang gshin rje rgya mtsho nor sbyin la 'char 'gyur/ 
13b3(rgyud): slar yang drug phyogs me dang lha min rlung dang dbang mtshams rim pa dag gis so// drag po gar nas nub 'gro'i nyin mtshan dbang gis byang du byed kyi nyi ma la chu nas me mtshams nges
13b4(rgyud): par de 'gro nyi ma 'dir gnas pa ni lho ru'o// dashar nas thun mtshams phyed nas rlung du rab zhugs de bzhin du ni nga lho ru'o// dbong ldan chu me nor sbyin lha min gnas su
13b5(rgyud): 'gyur te rlung gi nyi mar nub par 'gyur ba dang ldan rtsa ba'i sgra gcan dor nas phan tshun 'thab par rlung ni rnam rgyal ra/ ba tu 'gyur// g.yul du rtsa ba'i sgra gcan sgra spobs
13b6(rgyud): zos te de dang mnyam pa gzhan ma med// dbyangs dman 'thab mo ba ni mnyam dang mi mnyam yul du lhag pa yi ni bcom pa'o// dbugs kyis gnyis kyi ming gang snying kar rab zhugs de ni rtsod pa
13b7(rgyud): rgyal bar 'gyur// pho nyas dang pos mi brjod de ni rnam par rgyal ste phyi'i ming ni 'joms par byed// a ya yi ge dbyangs sogs rnams ni mnyam dang mi mnyam gnas kyis 'bras bu med par sman
13b8(rgyud): dus ni 'thab mo sa ru rgyal ba rnams ni g.yas dang g.yon du gal te mun can gyur na/ g.yul du seng ge drag po dang bcas lha mgon po rnams kyis ni bcom// rgyu skar sa la gsum du byas
14a1(rgyud): nas thub bzung rnams bcom dbang po nor sbyin rgya mtsho gshin rje la// 'khor lo da ni 'khor zhing nyin mo 'gro ba'i dbang gis ma lus rtag par rig par bya// rgyu skar gang la dus ni mun can
14a2(rgyud): rab 'bab gnyis pa'i lha ltung ba'i// g.yul du dgra'i ste na myur du ltung 'gyur lto ba'i nang du rgyal bar 'gyur// sgra gcan dus la gnas rnams stobs rnams shi bcas ltung ba mnyam par 'gyur lhan
14a3(rgyud): las 'byung ltos 'gro 'gro ba'i dbang gis de ru sde rnams bcom pa'o// lta ba'i cha spangs rnam pa gnyi ka mngal bzhug rnam par rgyal bar rab tu 'gyur// 'di ltar dpal ldan rtsa ba'i sgra gcan
14a4(rgyud): bla ma'i gsung du gnas pa'i dus kyi 'khor loro shes par bya// de'i phyir dpal ldan rtsa ba'i sgra gcan khams gsum las rgyal 'khor lo drag po lha min las// 'khrug dus du sa'i dkyil
14a5(rgyud): la gnas shes bya gzhan na dgra rnams med// rnal 'byor ma rnams 'jug pong drag po gza' tshogs dang / khanas dbyangs bcas gar de rnams dor nas sred gsum rgyal brgyal po rnam
14a6(rgyud): kyis gcig pu bzung bar bya// gang gis nyi zla zos nas lha rnams 'jigs byed drag po'i sman dang 'dra ba// sa'i shar dang nub tu 'khor zhing nyin mtshan dus su lto dang byang rnams dag go// 
14a7(rgyud): g.yul las dgra bcom blo bur dag tu rdzong dbus rgyal mu ni na ra ba zhugs na// phyi rol 'phrul 'khor byas nus rgyun mi 'chang ba'i rdo dang me 'dag rab tu 'phang ba dang // ral gre la sogs gcod pa'i
14a8(rgyud): 'khrul 'khor rnams kyis sa stengs gnas su 'dre ba rtsed dbye yis// rdzong de phyi mar byas nas nyin mtshan chu tshod kyis ni srang ba de ni sgrub par bya// bzhi ni brkyang gnyis khru ste mnyam dang mi mnyam rkar ba/ 
14b1(rgyud): gnas brgyad dag tu dbug par bya// ka ba lags thag gis bcings zung dang bzung ste rgyab tu gcig gis so// 'khrul 'khor rtsa ba'i tshad ni bcu dang lag 'gyur ste tshwa ni de'i phyed// srog shing khru gnyis
14b2(rgyud): dman par 'gyur te ka na ga yas sde chas lhag pa'o// zlum po phyed bcas khru gnyis thub bshed bu nges par sor mo dbugs gcig/ khru gang dor nas ka na yar ni srog gnyis rgyab kyi tshal phur gdab
14b3(rgyud): spyi bo 'og tu thag pa lnga bcus bcings sde chang byed kyis zlum po 'o// srog ging mtha' ru dkyil 'khor rab zhugs mtho// gang dag gi ni zlum por ro// srog shing sor mos khru gsum sprul// ldog
14b4(rgyud): nges par 'gyur zhing thag pa dang bcas nges par 'gyur// de dbus rdo 'ab bzhug 'dren byed stobs ldan rnams kyis thag pas 'then dA na// bkrol nas myur du na mkha'
14b5(rgyud): 'gre sde stong thog sgo gang bro bur lhung bar ro// ma lus phye mur byas nas sa sengs 'gro ste rdo rje dang ni ltung ba tsin na no// de'i sor phye 'khor los steng gnas su tshangs pa'i
14b6(rgyud): ri mo gzhog gnyis la// brgyad nyid 'ba' zhig gnas te lag gnyis mthil gi khu tshur bcings las rnam par grol// grol nas sa reg nges par mnyam dang mi mnyam rkang pa 'khrul 'khor lus
14b7(rgyud): gnas kyis// rang 'dod bde ba ltung 'gyur 'gro gsum dbang gis ma rjod ni nyams bya'i don byed do// gang gis rgyab na glang chen myur du ltung 'gyur na phran tshegs smos ci dgos// rdzong gi snyed yang
14b8(rgyud): gang zhig gnas pa'i dgra stobs ma lus phyi rol gnas lhung byed// de dang lhan cig mtshungs pa gang sde sa stengs gnas su bzhug 'gengs rnams la rdzong 'thab pa// rdzong der dgra gang gshin
15a1(rgyud): rje kha ru bzhugs kyur gang du 'khrul 'khor gis spun pa'o// gab drug drug gis ni las 'gyur gnyis 'byor mnyam pa khru bzung mtha' ru'o// snying po re re nyi sbyor gnyis dang / 
15a2(rgyud): mnyam lhag ma'i dman pa nyid ma yin// le tshe thams cad so so'i ra shing la ko ba sngon 'i gos kyi bze// dus rgyud skyon ga slong po 'am ni nyin byed gsum dag gis ni 'khrul 'khor gcig na
15a3(rgyud): tu bya// gnyis gnyis snying po'i mtha' ru lag pas g.yo ba 'am// kun nas rgya yas gdub// rgyab tu skye ba drug ste lag gnyis mnyam pa mngon du 'khrul 'khor mnyan pa rnams// khron pa ka
15a4(rgyud): bas bcings la rlung yab kyis ni spyod pa 'am yang ngan rdung nyid kyis/ de la rang ste gnas te chu gter la 'khro chu rdzong nyams// par bya ba'i don ched do// gnas gtsug mnyam rgya mtshol
15a5(rgyud): mtshams su rlung yub g.yo ba kun du ka bas bcing // rgyab nas mi rnams sa g.yo ba thag pa'i sa ni steng du 'gro/ rlung gis nges par nam mkha' song ste rdo rje steng du yi/ de nas
15a6(rgyud): me sgrol til mang 'phangs nas dgra'i stobs ni sreg par byed cing rdzing rnams thams cad do// 'khor l-i'o rtsa bar ze chun rab 'gyur ka na ye'i mdun du 'khor lo gzhan ma'o// sor mo gnyis
15a7(rgyud): gnyis mtha' ru brtsibs kyis kyang mdzes/ kun nas dkyil 'khor rtse mor ro// 'khor lo byed bcas khru gnyis 'gyur te kan ya'i phyed kyis srog shing gzhun ma de// srog gi rtse mor ral gri
15a8(rgyud): rnon po 'khor zhing nges par de yis 'khrul 'khor rtsa ba 'khor bas so// thag pas rlung gi 'khrul 'khor nam mkha' 'gro ste rang gi gnas nas rim pas so// rdzong ste dgra'i khyim du nges par sor
15b1(rgyud): 'gro bar radzag pa'i tshed byas nas sa'i tshad ni nges par de yis brjod 'gyur dgra rnams rtse mor dang gis 'khrul 'khor byin nas dgra'i gnas khyim gi 'og tum ni rab sbyin bya// 'khor/ 
15b2(rgyud): lo'i steng char lcags kyi gser bu dang shing rnams kyis khyim chen mdzes par byas// kun nas zlum po gzugs te shing lo ba dang ni ma he'i ko ba rnams kyis gdab par bya// mi rnams
15b3(rgyud): kyis spyod mnyam pa'i sa la 'gro ste ci srid 'obs kyi bar du'o// 'obs de gang bar byas nas rdzong gi rtsig pa dang ni sgo myur du rab 'jug byed// gnas la gzer bu gnyis kyis nges par
15b4(rgyud): gzhu rgyud mda' mnyam mnga' 'am mde'u rnon po rnams// g.yul gi dus su 'phangs na bu ram dang bcas glang chen phug nas rab tu 'gro// ka gnyis sa'i snying por bstan
15b5(rgyud): par btsugs te thag par yis ni rnam par bcings// thag pa'i dbus su thag pa mang po bskor nas zlum po dang bcas ral gri tshangs par zhugs// de dbus gri'i tshangs
15b6(rgyud): bar rab 'gyur nges par g.yo min phur bus gdab// phyag rgya skor ba dang ral gri 'dzin 'jug cha ru rangs par byed de/ steng bug pa'i ri mor 'gyur zhing shing leb 'byung ba'i
15b7(rgyud): g.yo ba la ral gri'i rtse mo'i dbus kyi cha ru lcags kyi byas pa yang ba'i zla ba gcig sbyin bya// zla ba'i steng du gang gis rkang pa'i blo bur ram myur de ni ral gris gcod par byed/ 
15b8(rgyud): rdzong sgo'i mthar dang mi bdag gnas su 'khrul 'khor 'di nyid kyis bdag/ snying po phyed ni rtsa ba'i gnas gyur nyi ma'i 'khru yis 'khor lo'i phyed kyis dgu cha'o// mtshams kyi ka ba
16a1(rgyud): ljags thag gis ni mnyam dang mi mnyam shing rta gnas nas phyed bcas tshad kyis so// chu phyed kyis ni 'thab mo'i sa stengs mnyam dang mi mnyam rta glang chen dbang gis
16a2(rgyud): phyed bcas khru ni gnyis su'o// lha rnams gnas ni rta dang blang chen rnams kyi'o// de nas 'khor lo'i phyed sa'i steng du mye long do shul rgyal mtshan la sogs rnam par mdzes// byed
16a3(rgyud): bcas gcig gnyis cha gsum ri bong lhag pa me ni rtsa ba'i gnas kyi lcags thag rnams phyed bcas cha gcig gis zlum po pad ma'i shing rta'i sa ni dga' ba'i dbye bas mnyam pa yin// 
16a4(rgyud): phyed bcas rtsa bas rtsibs kyi 'khor lo tshad steng rta dang glang chen dbang gis phyed bcas khru gnyis su'o// lha rnams pad ma'i rigs te lta bu rnams bcas dag pa'i rigs kyis
16a5(rgyud): ma rnams la// brgyad dang chu rter mig gis 'khor los rnam gsum 'di ru shing rta chen khyod dang mnyam mo// nyi ma'i mdzesapa 'khor lo gcig ste mi mnyam rta'i shing rta'i lha
16a6(rgyud): min ni rnams la nyams par byed/ 'thab mor phyed mi ldog 'gyur mnyam dang mi mnyam dang mi mnyam shing rnga che ni rgyal po'o// byed / sngon du yin te mnyam dang mi mnyam g.yul du rgyab tu
16a7(rgyud): bcom pa mnyam pa yin// drug lnga rgya mtsho me chas ka ba'i mtha' mnyam bug par rab tu 'gyur// rtsa ba'i steng du cha gnyis 'gyur zhing khyim gis mchi med g.yas khang / 'di ltar sar ni rgyal
16a8(rgyud): po rnams la pu ra rnam gsum dbang gis 'gron bgrod dus ston la// khru nas khru mthar phyogs kun la ni skor khang dag du 'gyur// 'khor phyed rtsa ba'i steng du rnam gsum bu ra'i dbang gis
16b1(rgyud): phyogs kun la ni 'chang ma'o// brgyad gnyis rgyang ste dbyed phyogs dus dus ni lag pa'i rten 'dis gsum la/ steng dang 'og tu 'khor zhing lag pas bzung ba'i ka na yur ni bud med gdun// 
16b2(rgyud): phyi dang nang du gnas yin steng 'og tu gnas pa phyogs brgyad g.yo bar byed// steng 'og tu 'khor lo'i sbubs su 'gyur zhing sgyur gyi rnam pa 'khrul 'khor lo kun nas so// sbubs kyi rtse mor
16b3(rgyud): bum pa'i gzugs ni khong stong 'gyur te sbubs kyi bu ga pa'i tshad yin no// chu ni 'gugs par byed de g.yo ba'i chu ni// hU~M bum pa'i bug pa nas dgrol bya// skyed tshal ldum ra rwa 'gyur zhing man
16b4(rgyud): pa'i sa ni gang dang gang du khrod pa'o// sngon brjod dang po'i sangs rgyas las ni gsum bla mas zla ba bzang la ni thams cad gang / de 'bus cung zad yul 'dir gsal bar
16b5(rgyud): dag gis das bstan pa'o// nga gnas su byu 'di kun shig zhes yang chags pas ma yin nyi 'an ma mamyong bas byung ba'i sa gnas su ma
16b6(rgyud): sa ni yang dag pa'o// dpag na 'bum phrag gsum la mo'i bdag po nyi ma'i dum burim pas 'khor// dum bu btsug na nor 'dab dang bcas dpagra cha gang zag nyi shu lnga dag go// de dbus
16b7(rgyud): mchog gis gangs ris sor bu'i kyil sa dzar/ seM la gangs ri dang las smye la sa'i rnam bu de'i sum kun rgyas so// phyil 'dab ma rnye re sbyin byed su pa dang phreng dang yul rnams kyis ni rgyun
16b8(rgyud): gangs byed pa chu cog gnas yin bya ba'i grong gnas sam 'apal zhes bya// bye ba'i grong gis sko ba'i tshul du 'gyur zhing grong 'dus gis ni 'o// gcig gnyin po tu
17a1(rgyud): brgya mtsho mda' re skye bo'i dbye ba lnga dang 'jig rten la sogs dbye ba yin// mi dang 'khor lo can ni tha dadang sa gnas 'khor le te de'i mkhas pas rdzal bya/ 'khor lo can dang
17a2(rgyud): gnyis min/ 'dus bu yul gi mi bdag log ban de nas gzhan// phyi rol dus kyi dbye bas ci ltar nges par 'gyur te/ 'gyur te 'gyur te 'jig rten mgon gi de bzhin no// 'od zer rdun
17a3(rgyud): dang gza' ni ri steng de bzhin thub pa snying / stobs lha'i skye gnas so// nyi dang ru sbal phag pa mi'i skye gnas so// seng ge dang bcas mi thub rje mi'i bu/ ram de bzhin nag po brgyad po de lha min rig
17a4(rgyud): la 'jigs ster rtul ni 'byung po'i skye gnas so// nyi shu rtsa gnyis sngan gi mtha ru lha min dgra ni phyag na 'khor lo rgya bar 'gyur// phyed dang chu bo ma yin phag pa ma lha min klu rigs ni gzhan
17a5(rgyud): rnams las mun pa'i lnga// 'di dkar po gro/ can snang ba dag srub pa gang zhig rgya pa de ni long ba yin// bsal b.radam pa'i yul gi ngag sbyin la sogs grong khyeram du ni
17a6(rgyud): bdun pa yang dag 'gyur gang du lha mini rigs dang / stobs ldan steng rje dang bral ze klo'i rnam pa yin// rnga mo \u0f7f dang bsad nasakhrag dang bcas pa dag ni bcos pa cung zad do// 
17a7(rgyud): ba lang shwa dang rdul chu mar dang tsha dang mnam lo ma 'bris dang sres// gcig tu mes bcos nags kyi 'bras bu dang bcas gang du me rnams kyi ni zas// btung ba mkha' 'gro'i sto ngar 'gyur te lAm/ 
17a8(rgyud): yin gi ste gnas mi dbang kye// thig le nus ma min sman nam lding chu bo mes sbyin 'dod 'jo dang // rdzong dang klog pang rig pa bzang po mi 'gyur che mchog lus med lha'i skad// kun chod 'di rnams
17b1(rgyud): gzugs kyi rgyal ba'i ye shes sku ni sa mngon 'jug go// 'das dang ma 'ongs da lngar byung ba'i rig byed rtog gi la so bstan bcos btsos ma lus smon// dpal ldan ka pa la bar ni nyi ma cung zad kyis ni sham
17b2(rgyud): pa zhes grags mi dbang kye/ phyogs bzhi ris skor ro yis rgya'i yon tan grags pa dpag tshad tshad// gnas su mi mchog bdag po lnga dbang bkod nas khyod ni bgrod gyis// dpal ldan shAkya'i rig
17b3(rgyud): la bsal bar mi dbang bdun ste dang ldan grags pa brgyad// 'di dpal ldan 'jam pa'i rdo rje lnga mchog gis bdud rdo rje'i dbang ni skur nas ma lus thub po'i rigs gcig dag tubyed meng dag ye shes/ 
17b4(rgyud): mngon lha min rig bsal// 'jig rten ster dpal ldan grags pa lag na mdun// sems can thar pa'i rgyu ru dus kyi 'khor las gsal por byed par 'gyur// de dbus nyi shu rtsal
17b5(rgyud): rims yongs su grangs pa sngan rnams dus kyi mtha' ru'o// rigs ldan rigs la lha dbang lha'i mchog gis phyag byas rigaldan drag por 'gyur mkhas rnams la zhi ba'i gzug
17b6(rgyud): te de bzhin kla klo'i rigs ni mtha' ru byed// ri'i rta zhon lag na mdung ste nyi ma'i 'od la dA 'khor lo can gis stobs dgra bcom// rigs ldan 'gas kyi dbus su lag pas dus grangs
17b7(rgyud): bu dang cha'o 'das pa dang / yul du kla klo'i chos ni rab tu 'jug par 'gyur// ji srid lha min dbang po drug pa lha mchog phyag byas drag po rigs ldan ji srid do// de dus nges par sa stengs
17b8(rgyud): gnas pa drag po gnyis la 'thab mor 'gyur ba yin// g.yul du lha min rnams ni ma lus sa gnas yan lag bzhi'i rang gi sdes bcom mo// dus kyi mtha' ru ke las ring lha mdzes gnas 'a
18a1(rgyud): los sgyur bar 'gyur bar 'byung / drag po phug po tshangs dbang khyab 'jug dang ni rigs ldan dang der 'grogs so// shing rta glang chen dbang dang gser gi shing rta rgyal po rnams dang
18a2(rgyud): lag na mtshon cha 'thab mo pa// rlung shugs ri rta yon tan gis bgrangs yon tan bye ba kha dog sna tshogs dang // rigs byed zhes bya 'bum phrag myos pa'i glang chen 'byung ba'i shing rwa 'bre
18a3(rgyud): brag go// 'khrug med drug med dgu bcu rigs ni gcod pan bcings pa mi dbang po ste 'di nyid kyis seng ge drag po dang bcas rigs ldan kla klo nyams par byed// mchog tu nyam nga ba'i
18a4(rgyud): 'thab mo pas ni kla klo tshogs bcom grang chen dpyangapos glang chen mo// ri rtas ri'i rta dang mnyam dang mi mnyam g.yul dus bdag rnams kyis sa dag go// rta rten sras chen po 'gram pa
18a5(rgyud): dang ldan mtshon marnon po rnams kyi bcom// drag ponakla klo'i dbang po mgon ma lus lha min bdag po blo byed drag po rigs ldan te// g.yul du bla bro bcom nas seng ge dang
18a6(rgyud): ni khyab 'jug dang bcas thams cad sde dang rigs ldan pa// ke las mi ring gshegs te lha mdzes gnas ni gang du 'khor lo can ni yang dag gnas// de dus sa la ma lus
18a7(rgyud): skye bo'i rigs ni bcos dang 'dod pa nor gis gang // 'brog tu 'bru rnams skyes nas btan pa'i 'bras bu'i drangs pa'i shing de rnams su 'gyur// kA klo'i chos ni 'khor bcas bcad nas
18a8(rgyud): yid bu lo rgya'i phyed la ni// lha mdzes gnas ni mtho ba ke la rgyab tu rigs ni 'grub par 'gyur// lha'i ma'i bla ma'i sras ni tshangs pa lha dbang bzung ni chos su 'gyur// rgyab kyi dus sku
18b1(rgyud): gcig la ma bdag tshangs par 'gyur te g.yas pa'i ru lha dbang ngo // srid gsum bla mas kla klo'i ma lus chos ni bcad par byas nas ni// brkyang rgyar lor gnas nas ni go 'phangs bde bar brgya
18b2(rgyud): te tshangs pa gzhag nas so// slar yang de dbus sras po kha dog dbye ba rnams kyis mi'i bdag por 'gyur// de rnams dbus su lha dbang mi bdag thub pa rnams dang gzhan rnams 'phel bar 'gyur
18b3(rgyud): kla k+ko'i nyams bya ched du dbang po bcu gnyis mngon du lhan cig lho rnams bdag po gshegs// dum bu dum bur kA klo'i chos bcom 'khor lo can ni bred ba'i go 'phang gshegs// lha mi bu
18b4(rgyud): ma'i rgyab dang mngon du sras po dag ni tshangs pad ga dang lha'i dbang po'o// rgyab du tshangs pa la sogs sna tshogs steng du ni du ma'i dbye bas 'gyur// tshangs pa la sogs shed
18b5(rgyud): bu'i lo ni brgya ni bcwo brgyad dang ldan mi rnams ni 'di nyid do// de phyed 'od srung gis te mchog gis steng gi ni mi'i seng ge'i de phyed do// de bzhin drug bcus dman par thun tshong
18b6(rgyud): ri rer mi thub la sogs seng ge'o// ci srid skal pa'i mtha' ru mi'i tshe ni lo gcig drangs brgya ru rab tu 'gyur// 'di ltar dum bu thams cad dus kyi tshod du kla klo'i chos ni 'jug pa
18b7(rgyud): rgya dang lo rgya gcig gnas de nas kla klo'i chos ni nyams pa yin de nas stong phrag nyi shu lag brgya yis dman ni pa ni sangs rgyas chos 'jug go// rdzogs dang gsum ldan gnyis ldan na
18b8(rgyud): brtsod pa'i dus te nus ma'i tshad kyis ru 'gyur// 'jig rten khams 'byung gza'i rgyu ba dang mnyam 'khor lo can ni 'byung ba dang // kla klo rnams kyi chos mchom mchog tu bde ba'i go 'phang / 
19a1(rgyud): rigs ldan la ni lam sbyin pa// 'di nyid thams cad ji bzhin de zla bzang khyod la dus gsum du ni bdag gis stan slar yang skye bo ma lus phan pa'i don dang thar pa'i rgyu ru khyod kyis bdag/ 
19a2(rgyud): la ci zhig zhu// dpal dang po'i sangs rgyas las drangs pa dpal dus kyi 'khor lo zhes bya ba la// 'jig rten gi khams kyi rnam par bkod pa ste// le'u dang po'o// 
19a3(rgyud): rgyal ba bskyed mdzad khyod kyis sna tshogs chung ni gang bstan bdag gis ma mtshal ba// slar yang nyan par 'tshal lo// srid gsum ma lus lus kyi dbus su ci ltar lags// zla bzangs tshig
19a4(rgyud): 'di gsan nas bde gshegs lagos zhes gsu dras nas rab gnas mdzad// sems can thar pa'i don du mchog gi thugs rje lus la sna tshogs tshad rnams dang // sa dang chu me rlung
19a5(rgyud): dang rdo rje lha gzhu rlung rnams dus kyi 'khor lo dang / nyi bza' sgra gcan lhun po gdengs ka mdzad shed bu lhag gnas 'khyo ga ba skar ma dang bcas pa 'pho ba zla phyogs nyin
19a6(rgyud): mo chos rnams ma lus kyi dbus su ni rnal 'byor pa yis stong pa'i dbye bas tso bo'i rnam gsum gnas ni rang rang yi ges shes bya lus 'dir khams tshogs ma lus ro drug zos
19a7(rgyud): shing btung ba las 'gyur zhing 'byung ba las ni ro drug nges par gsal ba nam mkha'i khams las 'byung ba'i tshogs// stong la ye shes rnam par sres na 'gyur zhing ro mnyam dang ni nam mkha'
19a8(rgyud): rtag pa'o// 'di ltar zhi ba 'byung bar gnas pa rnam gsum srid gnas rang gi lus la rig par byed// sa bon sa yis 'dzin zhing ro mnyam dang ni nam mkha' pad ma la gnas phyi nas chu yis skye
19b1(rgyud): byed pa yin/ me yis sangs par byed cing ro dang ro za rlung gis 'di yis 'phel bar byed 'phel na nam mkha' go skabs byin te dus kyi dbang gis de ltar 'grub po mi dbang kye// skye ba'i dus
19b2(rgyud): dong byis pa la sogs dus su lha'i gnas rnams byed do// sa bon las ni sa yis bsal bar lji par skye byed chus ni 'di ltar gshegs byed nyid// me yis smin par byed cing mchog gi rnam
19b3(rgyud): bcu rlung gis 'di ni 'phel bar byed// 'phel te slar yang nam mkhas go skabs byin te dus kyi dbang gis 'di ltar skye ba'o// / dngos po sna tshogs du ma lus bcos dgra dang yid ni nus
19b4(rgyud): ma rnams kyis spro bar byed// bsang ba'i chu skyes khrag gi dbus su srog dang bcas pa gal te byang chub sems ltung na nya dang rus sbal phag par 'gyur zhing mi'i seng
19b5(rgyud): ge mi thub pa dang // nag mo sangs rgyas mi dbang rnam bcur 'gyur te// 'di rnams kun ni gnas skabs bcu mngal du gsum yin// btsa ru dus de bzhin gcig ste byis
19b6(rgyud): pa'i dus yang ni nyis gzhon nu lang mam gzhan du 'gyur te rgyas pa gcig ni yang dag de bzhin gcig/ rgas pa nyid du ni gcig sring pa'i mnyam nyid mnga' nas skyes pa'i tha ma'o// nya ba
19b7(rgyud): dngos por nya rnams nyi ma cung zad 'gyur te ru sbal la ni'u sbal dngos po'o// phag par de nyid nyi ma skye mched 'gyur te mi'i seng ge la skye ba'o// me'u thung la byis pa nyid der ma la ni rgyal po/ 
19b8(rgyud): gnyis kyi so skye 'gyur// slar yang ma la 'gyur te de nyid nag po'i dus la rgyu ni bsal bar byed// sangs rgyas la ni zhing dang rtul zhugs nges par byed de rigs ldan 'chi 'gyur// rkang rus
20a1(rgyud): rtsa ni khu ba las 'gyur khrag las nges par pags pa khrag dang sha// mngal du bus zla ba gcig ni bdud rtse ror 'gyur sa bon khrag gis rab tu bskyed// phyi nas sa bon myug la/ 
20a2(rgyud): rang sems rnam bcu shin du phra ba'i rtse// lte ba la yang brgya rnams rgyad gzhan ka lag kha'i steng nas grol tshad ni// zla ba gnyis pa rdzogs pa rka lag kha ni 'di ru cung zad snyan par 'gyur
20a3(rgyud): zla ba gsum rdzogs nas ni rka lag 'grin pa dang ni mgo ni mnyam par 'gyur// zla ba bzhi ni galag gdong par phra ba'i rtsa rnams mgrin pa'i gnas su'o// sha dang khrag dang rus pa ma
20a4(rgyud): ro me 'od dam pa ni lnga pa rnams dang ngo // zla drug la ni sha dang khrag dang tshor ba dag dang sdug bsngal 'gyur// thub pa mchog smin ma skra dang khu ba ni lhag ma'i rtsa rnams te// zla ba
20a5(rgyud): nyin bzhin gong bu skye ba spang pa dang ni mi stong pa mig gi grangs kyis so// tshigs dang rus dang ro lhan dri tshul na rgyang pa dag pa'o// bug pa zhes byar skye ba'i dus su mi zad
20a6(rgyud): sdug bsngal skye ba ba nas dag/ gis sngams mngal du dmangal ge sdug bsngal gi skye ba'i dus na byis pa dngos kyi sdug bsngal lo// gzhon nu lang bco la ni bud med nor bral nyon mo
20a7(rgyud): sdug bsngal chen pos gang rga bar mchi ba'i sdug bsngal dag ste slar ni 'gro drug 'jigs te dug 'bod rdzogs// gti mug sgyu ma'i 'di dag sdug bsngal nas ni sdug bsngal len par byed
20a8(rgyud): 'khor bar mi nyid brgya lam na ste slar yang chos ni blo rgya lam na// de phyir sangs rgyas chags pa dang po'i theg par 'jug pa'i dga' ba'i gnas kyis so// de bas dpal ldan rdo rje theg par
20b1(rgyud): mA lus sgom pa'i blo 'jug rgya lam na// de nas sangs rgyas nyid 'dod mchog gis 'phangs la 'jug par rga e ma'o// mngal nas yang dag sru ste skye ba'i dus nas so skyes pa yang chos
20b2(rgyud): kyi sku so rnams skyes nas rgyal ba longs spyod sku ru nges par 'gyur ro rgyal kye// de nas sprul pa'i sku ru brjod de nges par mi rnams 'chi ba'i mtha'// slar yang 'di ni shas dang rnam
20b3(rgyud): shes dbye ba yis ni mngal dang phyi ru rnam bzhir 'gyur// rnam shes zla ba nyi ma yang ni pad ma la gnas de ni mngal du dag pa'i sku// khams dang phung po rnam bcu 'byung ba rgyal ba'i chos
20b4(rgyud): skur 'gyur// de nas rna ba sgra sogs skyes pa yon tan dbang gis longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku ru 'gyur// de sgra bsogs skye ba'i dus la 'dir ni sprul pa'i sku// skyes nas gang zhig
20b5(rgyud): dbugs 'byung nges par de ni yang dag sgo ru 'gyuranyid/ de nas so skyes gang zhig tshig ni mi bsal ba yang de bzhi na chos kyi sku// de nas gnyis skyes ltung ba'i rgyal ba'i lo
20b6(rgyud): spyod rdzogs par 'gyur ro rgyal po kye// seM nas mche ba'i mthar ni rgyal ba'i bdag po la ni phyi'i sbrul skur 'gyuradang por 'dir ni mngal du dpal ldan spyi'i rdo rjer 'gyur te/ 
20b7(rgyud): gsung gi rang bzhin skye ba'i dus// so 'byung nges par thugs te slar yang 'byung nas skye ba ye shes rdo rje'o// shes dang mi shes 'dras pa nyid zlar bcas pa ye shes rdo rje lasngags kun// sku
20b8(rgyud): rje la srogs mngal nas skye ba'i rim pas stobs dang ldan par 'gyur// sa'i dbus su me ru 'gyur te sa dang rlung ni stong pa'i dbus so// rlung dang sa dag du ni rang bzhin med pa'i dngos po chu ru 'gyur
21a1(rgyud): sa'i rten ni chu ste chu'i 'bar yin 'bar gis yang ni rlung yin no// rlung gi stong yin ji ltar rten dang rten pa'i tshul du rab 'gyur mi dbang kye// lus mchog phung po'i rten ni 'byung ba/ 
21a2(rgyud): yin zhing / 'byung ba'i tshogs kyi rtsa rnams so// rnam pa bcu'i rlung ni rtsa rnams kyir 'gyur srog gi rlung ni sems las byung ba'o// sems de nyid ni rang bzhin gnyis kyi yon tan dbang gis
21a3(rgyud): rang bzhin dang bcas rang bzhin med// de gnyis rten ni gang zhig khams gsum pos phyag byas pa gang de kun 'gro gzhom du med par 'gyur// dri ni 'dzin po las byung yang ni me las ro// 
21a4(rgyud): ste gzugs khyams chu lus so// rlung las reg skye zhi ba las kyang sgrar 'gyur nam mkha' la ni chos kyi dbyings// rgyal ba skyed mdzad stong pa yis ni slar bzung rlung ni chos kyi
21a5(rgyud): dbyings kyis so// dri dang me skye gzugs ro// dag dang chu dang rog ni de bzhin sa rnams dang / sred gsum la gnas gzugs ni sa las 'grub dang 'du shes dag ni chu las
21a6(rgyud): 'grub par 'gyur// tshor ba me las des te 'du byed phung po de bzhin rlung las rab tu 'gyur// shes rnams shes 'dres te nam mkha' rdo rje dang bcas las 'grub de ltar ro// 
21a7(rgyud): khams dang phung po la sogs kun ni byang chub sems rdul la sogs sbyor las 'gyur// rna ba rdo rje'i rang bzhin sems ni nam mkha'i rang bzhin 'gyur ro mi dbang kyi// sna ni sa'i rang bzhin de bzhin du
21a8(rgyud): yang lce'i rang bzhin 'gyur// chu'i rang bzhin mig ste sred gsum la gnas rlung gi rang bzhin pa'o// de ltar rna ba la sogs kun ni rnam shes sbyor ba yon tan dbang gis 'gyur// lus mchog smra shes
21b1(rgyud): pa'i khams la nam mkha' las ni zhe sdang rdo rje'o// rlung las phra dog rdo rjer gsungs te de bzhin me la 'dod chags rdo rje'o// rang bzhin yon tan dbang gis dpal ldan rdo rje dang ni rgyal chu dang ni ste// gti mug
21b2(rgyud): rdo rje dag dang nang lag bshang rnams dang ni rlung dang chu mes rnam dag las 'gyur// thur sel ye shes khams las rnam gsum shes bya srog rlung stong pa las 'gyur dang // rlung dbus mnyam dang me las slar
21b3(rgyud): yang cher brjod chu ste de bzhin khyab pa ni// sa las klu dang ru sbal tshangs pa dang ni lhas sbyin nor las rgyal bzhi po rlung dang me dang chu dang sa las rim pas rab tu 'gyur ro// lha mi rnams kyi gtsug tor stong pa'i khas
21b4(rgyud): 'gyur ye shes khams kyang bsal ba'o// snying gi pad ma rlung gi khams te nges par 'bar ba'i me brjod mgrin pa 'khor lo// smin 'tshams 'khor lo chung ste nor dang mda' lte ba'i pad ma dag
21b5(rgyud): gis// rka lag tshigs dru chen mo chu dang me ste rlung rnams gsum gi drangs kyis so// rtsa bsogs 'byung ba lnga po yon tan gsum ges gtso bo rnams kyi rga lag ni// mthe bong la sogs
21b6(rgyud): sor mo bcu po gsum grangs tshigs kyi gzugs ni ma lus par// de rnams sen mo'i mtha' ru bzung slar yang sor ni/ de nyid gzhan gi dbye bas so// gzhan yang ba spu'i mtha'
21b7(rgyud): dang lus mchog de dang ni de bzhin khams gsang ba gtsug tor dang ni lte ba lhan cig skyes par rgyal ba'i sku ste rang bzhin med pa'i sku// snying kha'i 'khor lo chos skur 'gyur
21b8(rgyud): zhing spyi bo'i pad mar sprul pa'i sku// 'grin par longs spyod skur 'gyur yon tan gyis ni rim gis mchog lha// snying 'khor mgrin 'khor spyi bo'i pad ma yang ni chos dang longs
22a1(rgyud): snong dag pa'o/ lte ba dang ni 'gran bsang spyi gtsug sing khar de bzhin gtsug tor dbus su ni// ma dang rtse bo rim pas so sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje rnam par gsum du 'gyur
22a2(rgyud): 'khor lo rim chen nam mkha'i dngam chu skyes ral gri rdo rje dang bcus rigs drug go// de rnams sbeng 'og rtsa gsum nye zla me yi dbye ba'i go 'brang dbye bas go 'phang rnam pa gsum du
22a3(rgyud): bzhugs// lus la dngos po zhugs te mapa' bzhin nor mnyam dngos po'i lus dag go// rang bzhin yon tan dbang gis khams drong kha dog dbye bas rnal 'byor ldan par rig/ se \u0f7f
22a4(rgyud): gnag dang kha dog dmar po zhes dang dkar po sa zung me dang rdula'o// ye ges nam mkha' yang ni lus dang po 'i dbye bas sde dang ljang kun 'gyur// shes rab thabs ni/ 
22a5(rgyud): rus ngag dang rdu nga zag bcas rlung dang stu rdung rje ga stong pas so mchog sus la 'gyur rab lan nu rang sems nyid // banas ni m+b+ha zhugs pa
22a6(rgyud): rang rgyal rigs kyi dbang gis rang gi rang bzhin la sogs so// de ltar lha mo sangs rgyas dang bcas yul dang yul can dkyil 'khor la ni brjod par bya// sa ni stong phrag drug skye nyin byed kyis
22a7(rgyud): grangs dang ni dmangal gi dbus su byas nas su// mo rdzogs nas ni ri bong 'dzin pas 'phel// srong dang rnams 'phel bar byed pa'o// bcu gnyis lo nas nyi mas khams kyi 'phel ba dang ni rang
22a8(rgyud): lus la sbyor// nyin dang nyin du bzung grangs rim pas skye gnas rtsa rnams chang par 'gyur ba'o// dpal ldan 'byung ba dbang po rnam pa bcu las kyi dbang po lngar 'gyur ro// de'i tshad kyang lngar brjod don/ 
22b1(rgyud): tan dang bcas yid blo ngar 'dzin bzang mo'o// lus la de nyid 'di dag sred pa gsum gi gnas su 'di ni rtse bos zos phung po lnga dag srid pa rnam gsum gnas ngag nyid la sogs pa'o// 
22b2(rgyud): skabs dang gsher ba nges par chu ste breb la yang rlung nyid do// thug pa stong pa sru ba'i nus de lha'i rim mchog char 'bab pa 'dir ni bdud rtsi'o// rdo rje sgra dang gzhu'i dri chen yang sner+tha/ 
22b3(rgyud): rjod dbugs 'byung 'jug gis bzung // zung 'di dgu rgya nyis ltab kyis ni 'pho ba gcig yin skar rtsis bug pa'i dbye bas so// rgyu skar so'i 'phreng nyid de nyi bzhin nu chod tshogs kyis
22b4(rgyud): phye bar 'gyur// ca ni chu bo rgyu ma smin te gzhan mra ri bong cha dang khams rnams ngo bo gnyis// ba spu shig dang lu bA srin bur bcas pa 'byung po'i ste gnas rnam pa bzhi/ 
22b5(rgyud): nan tan la sogs the bong tshigs te pad ma spyi bo lte ba'i pad ma'i nus ma'o// tshangs sgong g.yul sa mtho' ris 'jig rten mchog lag rkang pa 'jig rten stong dang 'og
22b6(rgyud): dag go// rgya mtsho gling ri gsher dang 'jam pa sra ba rnams ni khams rnams gsum ngang ngo bo nyid// 'dir ni dug mchog rten te mi g.yo dkyil 'khor khrag dang pags pa'o// rgyal po kye/ 
22b7(rgyud): ma lus skya ni grub pa yon tan srid gsum gnas nas du ma'i dbye bas grub pa'o// snying mgrin pad ma'i lte bar rdo rje nyi ma mes ni rim bzhin rab 'pho ba gzhu'i rnam pa bzlum dang nyi ma dang
22b8(rgyud): nyin dus me ni rgya mtsho zur gi thab khung la'o// de rnams steng na mchog gis me ni pad ma ltar 'bar ye shes sku ni mun can mtha'// gang du me dang zla bza' rgyu skar logs 'od ni mi 'byung bar
23a1(rgyud): gza' ni snying gis pad ma'i 'dab ste brjod pa'i chu tshod lte ba'i pad mar drug bcu'o// sprin dbus nyin mtshan rkang pa shed pu yang ste long spyod 'khor lo rgyu sbyar rgyal po kye/ rgyus
23a2(rgyud): chu tshod dag ni lte ba'i pad ma rnal 'byor pas rig bya// rtswa dang chu sa srang gsal la ma lus dang rkang pa'i tshigs rnams te// lte dbus chu skyes nyi ma 'dab mar mchog gi 'khar rim pas
23a3(rgyud): rgyu'aphro ba srog la zung dgu rgya nyes 'gyur gyis te rigs ldan dus 'byor rgyal po kye// gang dus dus 'byor dag la nyin mtshan rgyu ba der ni de rig bya// dus 'byor tshed dang nor
23a4(rgyud): sbyin pa mnyam pa g.yas g.yon rgyu ba shes par bya/ pad ma'i 'bar me'i rer nub dus ni rgyal byang chub tu ni chu yin no// me ni g.yas ste shar du 'bab pa'i rlung dang pad ma'i dbus su song
23a5(rgyud): 'pho ba lnga'i dbye bras dbugs 'byung dman pa drug bcur nyi shur rab tu 'gyur// de ltar 'phyo ba'i dbye ba nyid dang nyin bzhin dus su dus 'byor dbye bas 'gyur// stong
23a6(rgyud): bral sogs de nyid lnga ni nges par byed dur+g+ha zhing sa la sogs pa g.yas// sgra gcan mra zla nyi ma bza' lag/ skyes lha man bla ma sngags pa dang // rkub dman pa mkha' sogs
23a7(rgyud): dkyil 'khor la ni go 'phang bcu po zhing can no// zla drug zla ba dbang phyug 'gyur ba brang gi phyogs te lhur ni nyi ma mi dbang kye// de steng snying ka'i gnas te pad ma'i nor gi 'dab mar rtsa'i
23a8(rgyud): 'khor lor gnas// srog sogs pa'i rlung gi tshogs dang nyi zla me ni g.yas dang g.yon pa dbus su'o// g.yon pa rtsa ni ri bong can dkar 'dab ma yang ni g.yas su nyi ma khrag dag go// 
23b1(rgyud): dbus su dus me gzugs kyi bi shur dbugs byung dman pa drug bcu rab tu 'bab// nor 'dab pad mar srog ni 'jug mnyam gnas ched du brjod pa'i rlung dang ni// 'jug pa klu dang ru sbal chungs
23b2(rgyud): brlung ste lhas sbyin dang ni nor las rgyal 'di dag rnam bcu'i rlung ni// rtsi 'khor lo las kyi dbye bas yang dag gnas// lug spogs nas ni dung can mtha'i rtsa'i 'khor lo ma lus rang snyed
23b3(rgyud): pad ma la// nyi ma'iri brong lam zhugs srog gis srog byed gza' dang btung ba sa lus pa ni 'jug par 'og tu khyer zhing ma lus mnyam khyer zhing // phyed kyi lus la skyed dang kha dang lag pa
23b4(rgyud): rkang pas klu drang gar byed do// khyab pas 'ams byed rang bzhin yon tan dbang gis de bzhin lus ni 'dzag bar byed// klu yis sregs pa nyid de rjod dang rka lag sbrum pa ru stsa
23b5(rgyud): rlung gis so// sangs bcas rlung gis su lus 'khrugs dang 'khrug ste// lha min gris ni bla klo shi 'gyu lus kyang nor rgyal drung cig gis ni 'dor bar mi byed rgyal po kye/ 
23b6(rgyud): de ltar rlung srogs thams cad rang bzhin yon tan la gnas rlung rnams 'dor mi 'gyur// ser skye'i phra ba lug srogs lam gsum la gnas snar ma gang po che'i lde// rgyal ni drug se rnam
23b7(rgyud): rgyal 'gro ba yang ni nor skye dgu pa sku pa ku ta ha dang // phyogs kyi grangs kyi dung can ma gang byang chub sa bon bde ba'i mthar ni rab tu 'bab// dpal ldan rtsa ba'i 'khor lo 'di ni tshogs gos
23b8(rgyud): dbye ba du mas rnam grangs mang du 'gyur// dbang po me dang gshin rje bden bral chur bcas zung dang gnod sbyin drag dbus su// 'di rnams gnas su nyin mtshan du ste nyid gzugs kyis sten
24a1(rgyud): 'gyur ba'o de ste 'grin par gnas su gza' tshogs bcas pa rgyu skar 'khor lo gnas// tshangs yul dpal ldan 'phel ba dag dang dbyangs bcas pa las thig le dkar po/ 
24a2(rgyud): 'dzag/ rtsa bar sa dang g.yon du chu ste g.yas su me ni rab 'bab steng du rlung dag go// gnyis kyi dbus su nam mkha' dang ni sna phug rim pas bi shur rab tu 'bab// 'di rnams nus sam
24a3(rgyud): phug ste bcu gnyis mtha' dang cha'i mtha' ru mchog gi go 'phang 'gro// zhing na lag dag dang lag pa'i pad ma'i 'the bong ma lus mtha'// 'khor lo can dang rdor can rang gis lus
24a4(rgyud): la lha mchog bdag po yan lag bcu gnyis 'gog/ yang dag ye shes rigs ldan glang chen rta dang shing rta 'khor ni 'phags pa'i tshad// drag po so so'i ming du 'gyur te ha nu
24a5(rgyud): man ta nyan thos srog chags so// kle klo dbang po snang ba sdig sde gang zhig mi dge lam ni blo byed sdug bsngalaskyer/ a yAng tha ma ldanyan ma rig pa sde ma lus lha mno smras
24a6(rgyud): ni bdud de rnam pa bzhi// de du rtsod pa nyams pa sri de'i 'jigs pa zad de dpal gi rgyal ba thob pa'i lam/ ke le'i sar ni chos kyi sbyin pa byin par sred pa 'jigs 'jon
24a7(rgyud): nor rnams rdzogs pa'i sa// gang zhig mi nang ma'i bla ma'i 'dun rgyab sras po tshangs pa lha dbang po// srid gsum rnam rgyal 'jam dpal 'jig rten 'gon ni dbang ldan rdul dang byang chub
24a8(rgyud): sa bon no// sna tshogs sa stengs rgyab tu tshangs pa la sogs rigs ni du ma dag pa'i sangs rgyas sogs// de ltar kla klo'i dbang po nges par thob 'gyur lus can lus kyi dbus su'o// phyir
24b1(rgyud): ni rgyu tshul mkha'i yul du nges par kla klo 'khrug pa'i 'khrug ma yin// dus kyi lo ni me grangs nyin mtshan tshogs kyis sbyar te// bgrod pa'i yan lag las ris drug sum bcu'i cha thob
24b2(rgyud): ro yis bgrangs pa'i lo ni rnal 'byor ma rnams rigs// gza' yis bcad nas thob pa'i dus kyi 'khor lo'i lha ru nges par brjod pa'o// phyogs kyis bcad ba lnga dang lha mo rnams kyis
24b3(rgyud): mngon brjod 'gyur ro mi dbad kye// rig byed bug pa'i dbye bas nyi ma'i yan lag la sgyu 'phrul dra ba rnam gsum 'gyur/ slar yang 'byung ba rgya mtsho yin zhing me dang rgya mtshos dpal
24b4(rgyud): ldan dus kyi dus dbye ba// de nyid zhes bya drug gi dman pa gzhan yang 'gyur te byed kyi dbye bas tha dad pa slar sres gnyis dbye gsum bcu dgu dang phyogs kyi bug
24b5(rgyud): pa de nyid dang bcas po// nges par nyin rtsibs zla ngo'i cha la nyin drug gang zhig gza'i cha'i snyed// de na rdo rje can gi phyag/ rgya drug skye nyin mtshan tshogs gzhan sku gsung thugs kyi phyag
24b6(rgyud): rgya'o// shes rab sku la dus 'byor gsum brjod nges par rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud// nus me 'khro bos rim bcu drug rab 'gyur lnga ni sangs rgyas lha mo rnams dang mig sogs drug ste gzhan yang lha'i cho
24b7(rgyud): ni drug gnyis mi dbang kye// rnal 'byor ma klu gtum mo zhes bya rgyang srid pa 'di rnams kun ni yon tan gnyis// 'di nyid dpal ldan dus 'khor bzhis lhag rgyang dang de'i phyed na khams gsum pa lnga'o// 
24b8(rgyud): gang zhig nyi ma'i chal nyin bzhin nu tshong byung ba zla ba dbus las de rnams ma lus srid gsum gnas na rnal 'byor ma ste dus 'byor 'bres pas gnyis lta ba pa'o// nyin mos the dang nyin ma 'char ni yon
25a1(rgyud): gnyis kyang gang zhig rnal 'byor ma tshogs 'dir// ma lus gcig sdoms nyi ma'i nyin mtshan gsum du 'gyur ba mngon par brjod bcas 'gyur// zla bar phyogs kyi rab 'gyur nyin byed/ 
25a2(rgyud): ni lo'i dbye bas ma lus pas// 'di dag dang po'i sangs rgyas la ni mkha' dpal ge pa rgyal pos lha dang lha mo rnams// shes rab thabs nyin dang mtshan mor 'gyur te nyin phyed mtshan phyed mnyam pa'i cha/ 
25a3(rgyud): gang gis nyin mtshan dus dang zla ba'i dbye bas rang gi lus la shes// de ni dpal ldan 'jam nor srid pa'i 'jigs 'joms skye ba 'di nyid sangs rgyas so// de la sum bcu'i cha yis gsum ges nges par
25a4(rgyud): bgrangs pa'i dus kyi 'khor lo'i lho// phyir ni phyag rgya drug ste gzhan yang de nas 'khor lo'i rtse ni de bzhin no// gtsug tor rgya mtsho'i snying kur brgyad dang spyi bor rgyal po'i grangs ni 'grin par ro// lce
25a5(rgyud): bar yon tan brgyad po brgyad kyis bgrangs te rgyal po gnyis su 'gyur bar bsung dbus bgrangs// rtsa drug 'khor lo 'gog cing bcu yis yul 'joms 'dus pa'i ngo bos sa
25a6(rgyud): yang nas yang du nyis lngab bya ste sngar yang bgrangs pa'i 'khris pa'i ban kan rlung gi cha// 'di rnams nges par 'chi ba ster zhing bla ma las nges par dbang gis tshe dang nad med ster
25a7(rgyud): 'khor lo drug la dus sngo rnams nI 'chi ba'i 'jigs 'joms rnal 'byor la ngo mtshar med// brgya mtsho gtsug tor la ste 'phral bar brgya mtshos dus bcom pad kan khams ni bskyed
25a8(rgyud): byed pas// 'grin par song ste srang ka'i chu skyes mig gis drug bcom 'khris pa'i khams ni bskyed byed ma// rgya mtsho drug bcu lte ba la ste gsang bar rgyal po de bzhin rlung gi khams 'khru/ 
25b1(rgyud): pa/ gsang bar gzhan rnams phyogs drug gsungs pa rnams ni nges par 'dus pa 'gog pa'o// rtsa drug 'khor lo 'gog pa lam rnams gsung ngam gnas nyi zla me yi dbye bas so// srog
25b2(rgyud): chags rnams la gang zhig mchi ster bla ma la nges dbang gis lus la de rnams bsrung // drug la gal te srog zhugs gyur na srog chags rnams kyi 'tsho nges 'joms so// phra bor ma zhugs rnal
25b3(rgyud): 'byor rnams kyis 'chi ba'i yul ni 'bigs pa gang zhig yin// gal te nyin mtshan rtsa gcig las 'bab dus kyi lo ni ru 'tsho bar 'gyur// gal te zla phyed rgyun ma mchad par 'bab na mi rnams
25b4(rgyud): lo ni phyed bcas 'tsho// zla ba gcig tu rgyun mi 'chad 'bab pa zla gsum du mtsho mi dbang kye// de ltar rnal 'byorarang gis lus la zla bar spong ba'i 'chi ba dus kyi 'khor los
25b5(rgyud): shes nas nyi shu lngar ni nyi 'gro gnas pa'i skye ba lnga ru 'phel bar 'gyur// de nas gcig nas lhag ste gsung+ga gis bgrangs pa'i bcu ni gsum gis lhag pa nyid// rdzog
25b6(rgyud): dus nas den sum mig zla ba drug gsum zung dang zla ba gang // zla ba de rnams nyams pa'i lhag ma dag ni tshes dang phyogs mda' yon tan nyi zla srog gi'o// rang gi gnas nas cho ga ni cha yis 'byung gA/ 
25b7(rgyud): 'khor lo spong ste/ nyams dang lhag ma mnyam// lo zla nyin mo gsum mig zla ba dang ni drug gsum zung dang zla ba gang // rdzogs pa nas mi zad pa nyam zhing tshes phyogs mda' dang yon tan lte ba la
25b8(rgyud): ni zhugs// nyin mtshan sum bcu drug gi mtha' ru nyin phyed nyan la gnas pa'i bza'i rtsa ste rnams dbyangs la ni 'dzi nyin phyed rgyu zhing 'grod par 'bru'i 'debs pas so// phyi nas gcig nas lhag pas
26a1(rgyud): rgyu zhing nyi dang nyin bzhin nyid kye lo'i bar du'o// 'chi ltas sbyor bas 'chi bar 'gyur// dad pa mtha' me 'jig rten nyin mtshan tshogs ni nyi mas lo gsum dag nas 'dor/ 
26a2(rgyud): de nas gnas bcas mnga' dang dus ni ngas par 'dzin tri ma dAl dang ri zla gsum bral mo// rmig sbrul du mtha' dang ni nor dang lag pa gzhan te bdun pa dag la gnas// de nas ches
26a3(rgyud): bsogs thams cad nyin tshogs gang ni de ltar lci ba ci srid nyid// ci srad dus kyi lo nas mi gcig le nyin mtshan 'gro ba gnas shing yang dga' pho// zla ba zhes dang nya ma'i lam la mnyam
26a4(rgyud): dang mi mnyam nyin mtshan gcig gi rim pas 'phel// slar yang 'phro ba'i dbye ba mnyam dang mi mnyam nyin mtshan gis ni bcu gnyis rtsibs su byas// ji srid zla ba phyed dang gnyis
26a5(rgyud): par gzhan ni gsum lngapa bcu ste 'tsho ba'i nyin mas na gsum// dbugs ni nu'i srang dang rtsa dang nyin mtshan dus las de ni rim par gnas// lo bdun bgreng ba'i yus
26a6(rgyud): kyis drug bcu'o// sum bcu lo zla gsum las nyin mtshan 'gro ba'i dbang gis lo dang phyogs gsum gris dusakyi 'khor lo ni sum bcu rtsa gnyis byed bcas bcom zhing nyin
26a7(rgyud): mtshan tshogs bcom zhing nyin mtshan tshogs bcom zhing gnas par 'gyur// chus ni sbrul sbyar lte ba'i 'khor lor phyogs dang phyogs kyi rtsa ni 'chang // tshigs re re'i rtsi ni me'i nyin mtshan
26a8(rgyud): gis dor las kyi 'khor lo dang bya zhes bya ba las// 'grin par rgyu skar rtsa ni nyin dang nyin du zlo ba'i nang du rim par 'dor// thig le la gnas phyogs nad zla ba'i bar 'dor// lo bcad nas
26b1(rgyud): ni phyogs kyi dbus su dbyangs dang nyin mtshan dbang gis skye ba zad do// nyin dang mtshan gi dus su dbugs 'byung 'jug pa chad pas 'tsho ba'i nyin ma gcig lte 'grin bral ba dag ni rang gi
26b2(rgyud): sring pad mar rtswa'i rnams de'i lhag min// nyin mar raM dang me'i gnas rang snying pad mor byed bcas rtse skye de bzhin no// na lag tshigs ni rjes kyis dus bgrangs de bzhin nyid mthu
26b3(rgyud): gi bar du nyid do// mthar ni rnam pa thams cad 'phra rab tshul 'beb pa nyin mo snying gi pad ma spangs// stong phrag sum bcu rtsa drug lo rgyu'i nyin mtshan tshogs kyi sa ni gnas pa'o// gang
26b4(rgyud): rdzogs pa nyin mtshan dus su nyi zla rang rang tshul gis nus ma yin// nyi ma nyin mo nyi ma rgyu bar sbyin par yang 'gyur zla bar de'i phyed rgyu skar nyin mtshan rab dbye nyi zla'i// tshul de ste/ 
26b5(rgyud): stong pa'i zla bar 'chi ba'o// lus srog lhag ma gang ni gzhu'i rab tu brjod pas rkang pa reg byed kyi dman/ pa drug bcu'o// 'pho ba'i dbye bas nyon bzhin dus su rtsa'i
26b6(rgyud): zung ni rab tu 'joms pa'o// slar zhing lo'i dbus su nyi zla spyod phyir stong pa mig dang ri grangs so// dus kyi lo ni rgyu ste lce dang mi rnams kyi tshad ni rang rang tshod kyis so// gal ta mi rnams
26b7(rgyud): dus kyi rtsa la zos par nad dang snun par gyur na ni// de la rten te myur du blo myur du ni zhugs te rtsa ba'i 'khor lor dus 'khor lor ma'i ni 'gogs nas nyi ma'i spyod pa'i bcad nas ma lus
26b8(rgyud): pa/ dbus su phra mo'i rten pa gang zhig srog chags rnams kyi srog ni 'phrog go// mi dbang rkye/ snying bad dpal ldan bral bar ri bong rkang 'gyu 'byung ba phyogs dang nyin zhes bya// longs
27a1(rgyud): spyod lta pa'i 'khor lor tshul bcur bcas drag po rlung dang rgyal zhes bya// de nyid zhes bya mtshan bdun 'dor te thA ba rim pas zlog pas slar yang ngo // theg le rdzogs par
27a2(rgyud): byas te nag po'i phyogs la steng kar zhugs cing skye ba'i dus// slar yang nag por de bzhin 'jug skye nang pa nang pa nas ni lte ba'i pad ma'i bar// rgyud gnyis bcu drug sdebs te steng ka skye drug
27a3(rgyud): de bzhin dkar nag pad ma'i ming // 'grin par sum bcu gnyis rtsibs gzhan ni gnyis lngab dmar ser lte ba la/ brgyad gnyis lte 'grin la ste spyi bor snying ka spyi gtsug de bzhin dkar naH/ 
27a4(rgyud): pad ma'i meng / 'grin par sum bcu gnyis rtsibs gzhan ni gnyis lnga ba dmar ser lte ba la// brgyad gnyis lte/ 'grin lu ste spyi bar steng kar kar dang // nag po rdzogs pa ra
27a5(rgyud): a srogs sum bcu'i dbyangs gang ha ya ra ba la ldan thig le dpal ldan tsheg drag gis// phyin drug bcur 'gyur te dus rgyal por nor dang so ste de rnams ge sar rtser
27a6(rgyud): thig le'i rnam par chog gis ni pad 'dab mchog la ka sogs sde yis tha dad do// brgyad dang nyi shu la ni thun 'tshams 'gro ba'i dbang gis nyi mya gnas dang zad// phyogs dang zla bar rang
27a7(rgyud): rgyus nyin mtshan zhes bya'i rkang pa sbyin pa dag dang byed// slar yang zla ba gnyis kyis zhan pa'i nyi lo'i sbyor bas 'phel bar 'gyur ro// rdzogs pa'i lo nyin drug yin te gzhan yang 'chi ba'i
27a8(rgyud): 'tshams su de bzhin 'phel// de bzhin nyi mar gnyis lngab kyis 'phel 'di ni lo'i sbyor bas rgyal po kye// dbugs drug gis ni srang gcig rab 'gyur chu srang drug bcus kyang ni chu tsho/ 
27b1(rgyud): drug bcus mes nyin mtshan yin te nyin mtshan gsum gas bgrang sa pa bcu yis rtsu ba gcig/ zla ba drug gis ni bgrod yin bgrod pa gnyis pa nas no lo gcig dag tu grags te// lo/ 
27b2(rgyud): me rnams tshe ni sbyin par 'gro bar 'gyur ba dus kyi rtsa'i dbang gis so// 'jig rten gsum la nyi zla rang gi lus la rdzogs par byed nus pa'i lha lha min me'i rnal 'byor ba med dazla ba
27b3(rgyud): rang rgyus mi sbyong dang // nyi ma rgyu skar thams cad srid pa'i gnas su lo'i nang nus rim gis rgyu ba min// lo dang lo sbyin gis ni dus kyi 'khor lo dpa'o gcig po de yis srid pa zos// gral te
27b4(rgyud): rtse gcig tshang bar 'gyur na gtsun sbyar nyid du 'gyur ro/ mi dbang kye// de tsam mtshan mo lnga yis 'dor te mchog gi chas ni gong bu bcad pa'i dus su'o// rna ba sgra dang kha dang yis nges
27b5(rgyud): par ro 'dor mig dbugs su ni migo gi 'bras bu/ ste/ sna yis dri ste mi rnams kyis ni rkang pa lag pa lus kyi drod ni rim gis so// sna rtse 'phrang spyi bor lag pa zhag
27b6(rgyud): pa de'i rang bzhin dag tu mthong lag pa'i 'brel gnyis rgyu skyegs khu bas byugs na// 'di ltar dmar por ma byed do// nyi ma kha dog gnag dang rdzogs pa'i ri bong 'dzin
27b7(rgyud): pa kha dog ser por mthong // gcin dang lus ni grang bar gyur na de nyid nyi ma de nyid mchi'i mi dbang kye// lce rtsa spyad nag rab 'gyur mig la tshangs pa'i ri mo shin du phra ba'o// dbus ni nyi ma'i
27b8(rgyud): lam la de bzhin khur chos gnyis dag rab tu g.yo ba dang // mchan khung la zhugs nu ma'i steng du gza' tshogs thams cad 'phro ba dang bcas mthong // 'grin pa lus bcas rengs dang lus
28a1(rgyud): ni 'khor ba yang ni 'chi ltas 'chi mtshan no// skye ba tsal ba'i dus su byis pa gzhon nu gzugs te gang zhig byed pa ni zod pa 'jig rten la ni slar yang de nyid dus kyi 'khor lo can/ 
28a2(rgyud): giso byed ste nyi mas min// nyi zla la sogs lha rnams 'byung bar ldan pa mtshan mo'i cha la bcom ldan 'das de zos// slar yang dpag med dor de nyin mo'i dus su skyed pa'i don du rim gris dor / 
28a3(rgyud): sgra la sogs pa las drug 'gyur zhing byed pa dbang po rnams ni drug du 'gyur// lo zla phyogs dang nyin mtshan mo tshes dang nyi zla rnams ni byed pa po// de rnams sdud pa'i byed pa po bzhin 'di ru 'gyur te skyed/ 
28a4(rgyud): byed byed po byed ma yin// mkha' khyab nam mkha'i rdo rjecan ni yul bral yon tan bral zhing dngos po med pa'o// dri dang gzugs dang ro dang reg pas dang chu ste me dang rlung rnams ni gzug
28a5(rgyud): can nges par brgyad yin yang dag yul la 'byung ba'i rtsa po gcig po ma lus pa// ma lus pa 'jig rten gsum po 'di ni dus kyis dbang gis 'brel zhing nyams par 'gyur// stong pa
28a6(rgyud): chos kyi dbyings dang yid ni gzugs med yin zhing mi dbang kye// bdag nyid rang gis bcings te rang bzhin la gnas yon tan rnams kyis ngar gi srin bzhin no// bdag gis bdag ste gzhan yang rnam par
28a7(rgyud): tog yid kyis grol te/ phyer rang bzhin yon tan gnas pa'i rang gi las kyis bde sdug byed do rgyal po kye// byed pa gang gis myi zhig byed de rang bzhin rnam bral mi shes 'jig rten rmongs// sa mu me rlung nam
28a8(rgyud): mnga' son tan dag se bro rung du 'dzin dang sems rags dang phra ba gzhan ste son tan rnam pa gsum gnas yig thig le la sogs 'byos// rags la rags pa'i dpung po phra ba'i sems la rdza ba'i
28b1(rgyud): nga dag dang gnas/ ye ges sku ste rang bzhin kyi 'gyur ba'i sgrog ni 'gyur ba ma yin// ma gros stong pa lnga po rang bzhin mi 'gyur dpal ldan cha dang theg so smra// dus dang sems dang tho ste de bzhin/ 
28b2(rgyud): rang bzhin yang ni// dbyangs gzhan chung la sogs gsum gi yon tan bcu pos rags pa'i yi ge ste ni 'gyur ba bcu drug gzhan/ de rnams nang nas khyad byed ngo bo nyid med rang bzhin med dang ma bcom
28b3(rgyud): rdo rje can/ 'khor ba bde ba sdug bsngal rang bzhin yon tan la gnas las las skyes pa de spyod do// rags dang phra ba gzhan ste rnam gsum 'di dag mi rnams las su 'gyur bdag gi byed po khyab
28b4(rgyud): par las te gzhan yang phyogs la yod pa'i byed po zhes ni las/ bdag ni byed min bzhan pa 'am na// rang bzhin rnam bral las ma ni zhes de phyir gang zhig byed pa pos ni srog chags rnams
28b5(rgyud): la bde sdug ster dang 'phrog par med// gang zhig sngon las rnam gsum 'khor bu ru ni 'bras bu rab ser 'gyur/ rdong sa bro ni bsgyid bang srung byed do// bas/ 'di ru 'phrog pa
28b6(rgyud): ster ba'i/ dpag med dge ba rang lus la// pro ga puH/ pa rang mig gis mthong // bye ba 'dod pa'i nus dang rang med grol ges nus pa gsum pa'o// dngos bor snang ba rab 'jug ro mnyam byed
28b7(rgyud): ba don ni nye bar thob par byed// slar yang 'dor zhing srid gsum phyag byas bzhi pas gnyis su med pa'i rim las so// de rnams dbus su rdo rje can gis bza' dang / tsa'adir ba bcu zhig/ 
28b8(rgyud): med do// mi dbang kye/ bdag gis byed po bde dang sdug bsngal bster bar de la ni mi 'gyur rgyal po kye// sems nus rnam par spangs nas gang zhig bde dang sdug bsngal ster

281a5(rgyud): nang gzhan gsum bdag nyid can// dus kyi 'khor lo phyag 'tshal lo// rtag tu khyed lo skyabs su 'chi// dpal chen dang po 'chog gi sangs rgyas rtsa ba'i rgyud chen po nas phyung ba/ rtse

281b2(rgyud): dang / 'angadu byed drug/ rnam par shes pa kun nas nyon mongs pa'i chos can nam/ rnam par byang ba'i chos can sa/ chos can du yang dag par rjes su myi mthong po/ gzugs ni tshor ba dang lhan cig kun tu rgyu zhes bya
281b3(rgyud): ka byan rjes su myi mthong ngo // tshor ba kyi 'du shes dang / 'du byed dang / rnam par shes pa lhan cing kun tu rgyu zhes bya bar yang dag par rjes su myi mthong ngo // de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni 'di ltar chos gang
281b4(rgyud): du sbyang ljin cig kun tu rgyu zhes myong du/ 'a bzhin gas spyod pa'i phyir 'gro bskyed do// rnam par 'gror nyid myong ngo // 'du myed do/ rnam par 'du ba myed do// shA rang ti'i bu
281b5(rgyud): skyo gyi slong pa nyid gang yin pa de ni gzugs ma yin/ tshor ba'i stong pa nyid gang yin na de ni tshor ba ma yin/ 'du shes gi stong po nyid gang yin pa de ni 'du shes ma yin/ 'du byed
281b6(rgyud): gi stong pa nyid gang yin pa de ni 'du byed ma yin/ rnam par shes pa stong pa nyid gang yin pa de ni rnam par shes pa ma yin te/ 'di ltar gzugs gi stong pa nyid gang yin pa de ni thogs par myi byed do// 
281b7(rgyud): ba'i stong pa nyid gang yin pa de tshor bar mi byed do// 'du shes gi stong pa nyid gang yin pa de 'du shes su myi byed do// 'du byed gi stong pa nyid gang yin pa de mngon par 'du myi byed do// rnam par shes pa stong
281b8(rgyud): panyid gang yin pa de rnam par shes par mi byed do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sha r+ya dwa ti'i bu gzugs kyang bzhin ma yisu stong pa nyid kyang bzhin ma yin/ stong pa nyid kyang bzhin ma yin la gzugs kyang bzhin ma
